### [1] [GigaWorld-1: A Roadmap to Build World Models for Robot Policy Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02642)
*GigaWorld Team,Angyuan Ma,Boyuan Wang,Bohan Li,Chaojun Ni,Guo Li,Guan Huang,Guosheng Zhao,Hao Li,Hengtao Li,Jingyu Liu,Jiwen Lu,Qiuping Deng,Tingdong Yu,Xuancheng Xu,Xinyu Zhou,Xiuwei Xu,Xinze Chen,Xiaofeng Wang,Xiaoyu Tian,Yang Wang,Yifan Chang,Yukun Zhou,Yun Ye,Zhenyu Wu,Zhanqian Wu,Zheng Zhu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了世界模型用于机器人策略评估的关键特性，提出WMBench基准，分析7个视频世界模型、4种动作编码方案、超324,000次仿真rollout，得出长时域动作一致性比短期视觉逼真度更重要的核心结论，并据此构建了面向策略评估优化的GigaWorld-1模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具身机器人基础模型的评估存在瓶颈：LLM可通过数字基准高效评估，而机器人策略需要依赖硬件和人工监督进行缓慢、昂贵的真实世界rollout。世界模型作为替代策略评估器日益受到关注，但决定其评估可靠性的关键属性仍不明确。

Method: 构建WMBench基准（基于真实机器人遥操作数据和匹配的策略rollout，覆盖多种操作任务）；对7个视频世界模型、4种动作表示方案进行系统分析；完成超324,000次仿真rollout与真实机器人执行配对对比；引入CVPR 2026 GigaBrain挑战赛社区提交、合成轨迹及超12,000小时训练视频进行丰富分析。

Result: 得出三个核心发现：(1) 评估器质量取决于长时域、动作保真的rollout一致性，而非短期视觉逼真度；(2) 预训练收益不仅来自数据规模，还来自通用世界知识与机器人特定可控性的平衡；(3) 动作编码、记忆设计和面向评估的后训练等架构选择强烈决定与真实机器人行为的一致性。

Conclusion: 基于上述发现，提出了实用设计路线图，并实现为GigaWorld-1——专门面向策略评估优化的世界模型。完整开源代码、模型、数据集和工具包，以推动具身基础模型的可扩展评估研究。

Abstract: Evaluating embodied robot foundation models remains a critical bottleneck; unlike large language models efficiently assessed via digital benchmarks, robotic policies require slow, costly real-world rollouts limited by hardware and human supervision, which has driven interest in world models as surrogate policy evaluators, yet the key properties that make a world model reliable for policy assessment remain poorly understood. This work presents a systematic study of world models for robotic policy evaluation and introduces WMBench, a benchmark constructed from real-robot teleoperation data and matched policy rollouts covering diverse manipulation tasks to enable controlled comparisons across model families, action encodings, rollout horizons, and evaluation metrics. Using WMBench, we analyze 7 video world models, 4 action representation schemes, and over 324,000 simulated policy rollouts paired with real robot executions, further enriching our analysis with large-scale community submissions from the CVPR 2026 GigaBrain Challenge, curated synthetic trajectories, and a training videos spanning more than 12,000 hours. Our experiments deliver three core insights: evaluator quality is dominated by long-horizon, action-faithful rollout consistency rather than short-term visual realism; pretraining gains stem not only from data scale but from balancing general world knowledge with robot-specific controllability; and architectural choices including action encoding, memory design, and evaluator-focused post-training strongly determine alignment with real-world robot behavior. Drawing on these results, we derive a practical design roadmap and realize it in \textit{GigaWorld-1}, a world model specially optimized for policy evaluation, and we fully release our code, models, datasets, and toolkits to advance scalable evaluation research for embodied foundation models.

</details>


### [2] [EVA-Client: A Unified Data Collection, Inference, and Deployment Framework for Embodied Policies on Real Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02646)
*Heqing Yang,Yang Yi,Liyao Wang,Linqing Zhong,Donglin Yang,Ruipu Wu,Zitong Bai,Fengjiao Chen,Manyuan Zhang,Linjiang Huang,Si Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: EVA-Client 是一个开源框架，用于在真实机器人上部署、收集数据和评估已训练的操控策略。它统一了策略迭代循环中真实机器人阶段，采用组件解耦架构，支持可检查执行，并将每次评估同时作为数据收集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人策略在真实硬件上的部署、数据收集和评估流程往往碎片化，缺乏统一的代码库。每次评估运行通常只是形成印象而非可复用的训练数据，导致策略迭代循环中真实机器人阶段效率低下。

Method: EVA-Client 提出三项设计：(1) 组件解耦架构，将机器人后端、推理策略和传输中间件组织为正交网格，添加新机器人或策略仅影响对应层；(2) 可检查执行机制，提供 Debug、Collect 和 Eval 三种工作流，覆盖从开环仿真到连续实时控制；(3) 每次评估运行同时作为数据收集，以训练就绪格式记录完整 rollout，附带详尽日志和并排对比查看器。框架还将主要实时推理策略（同步/异步执行、ACT 风格时序集成、Real-Time Chunking、naive-async 消融基线）统一在单一配置界面下。

Result: EVA-Client 实现了在单一代码库中统一真实机器人部署、数据收集和评估流程，使得每次评估都能为下一轮训练提供数据支撑，而非仅作为无记录的印象。

Conclusion: EVA-Client 通过组件解耦架构、可检查工作流和评估即收集的设计，有效弥合了策略训练与真实硬件执行之间的鸿沟，为机器人操控策略的迭代开发提供了高效的基础设施。

Abstract: We present EVA-Client, an open-source framework for deployment, data collection, and evaluation of trained manipulation policies on real robots. Sitting between a policy server and the physical hardware, EVA-Client unifies the real-robot stages of the policy iteration loop within a single codebase. It makes three contributions. First, a component-decoupled architecture in which robot backends, inference strategies, and transport middlewares form an orthogonal grid: adding a robot or a strategy touches only its own layer. Second, inspectable execution through Debug, Collect, and Eval workflows, with modes ranging from open-loop simulation to continuous real-time control. Third, every evaluation run doubles as a data collection, recording full rollouts in training-ready format alongside exhaustive logs and a side-by-side comparison viewer, so each evaluation feeds the next round of training rather than ending as an unrecorded impression. EVA-Client further consolidates major real-time inference strategies, synchronous and asynchronous execution, ACT-style temporal ensembling, Real-Time Chunking, and a naive-async ablation baseline, behind a single configuration surface.

</details>


### [3] [MorphQuad: Morphable Quadrotor for Superhuman Maneuverability, Manipulation, and Resiliency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02764)
*J. Diaz Peon Gonzalez Pacheco,J. Xu,A. Zhao,H. Zhou,A. Navsalkar,A. Scheffer,A. Malli Reddi,S. Shankar,Y. Bao,V. Tzoumas*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: MorphQuad是一种可变形四旋翼飞行器，通过独立的双轴云台驱动每个旋翼系统，结合全局稳定控制与能量最优推力分配，首次同时实现了全向飞行中的最大推力矢量、全局稳定性和紧凑标准设计，从而具备极端机动性、操控性和抗扰韧性（MMR）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有空中飞行器无法同时满足三项关键需求：(I)任意方向的最大推力矢量以支持接触力施加和扰动抑制；(II)全局稳定性以实现任意姿态/位置控制；(III)基于四旋翼等标准平台的紧凑设计以继承既有技术积累。缺乏MMR能力限制了空中机器人在基础设施维护、接触式检查和应急响应中的应用。

Method: 采用硬件与控制协同设计方案。硬件层面，通过双轴云台独立关节化驱动四个旋翼系统，使每个旋翼可在两自由度方向上偏转；控制层面，提出全局稳定控制策略和能量最优推力分配算法，仅在避免下洗流干扰和万向节锁死时才允许旋翼间推力抵消。

Result: MorphQuad在完全机载自主的条件下展示了多项能力：多圈旋转同时平移或悬停（管道检查与目标跟踪）；以人类级别的力量完成阀门旋转、栖息、物体按压与推动（操控性）；来自任意方向（甚至针对单个旋翼）的风扰抑制及推拉恢复（抗扰韧性）。

Conclusion: MorphQuad通过硬件与控制协同设计，成功突破了传统空中飞行器在推力矢量、全局稳定性和平台紧凑性之间的权衡，首次在单一平台上集成了MMR能力，为空中接触式作业和极端环境下的飞行操作开辟了新可能。

Abstract: Infrastructure maintenance, contact-based inspection, and emergency response can benefit from aerial vehicles that act as a flying human hand with extreme maneuverability, manipulation, and resiliency (MMR): maneuverability to fly in arbitrary orientations to reach remote and tight locations; manipulation to point sensors, turn valves, and press tools at arbitrary orientations; resiliency to maintain accurate motion and force control despite disturbances from arbitrary directions, such as wind, ground effects, and friction. Realizing MMR on aerial vehicles requires not only omnidirectional flight; it also requires (I) vectoring of maximum thrust in any direction, to maximize capacity for contact-force application and disturbance rejection, (II) global stability, to enable control over any orientation/position, and (III) compact, standard designs that build upon platforms such as quadrotors to inherit technological know-how. No current aerial vehicle simultaneously enables I--III, due to structural and control limitations that constrain actuation. We present MorphQuad: a morphable quadrotor that enjoys MMR. Key to our approach is a hardware and control co-design: on hardware, we independently articulate each of the four rotor systems via two-axis gimbals; on control, we introduce globally-stable control, and energy-optimal thrust allocation that permits inter-rotor thrust cancellations only to avoid downwash interference and gimbal lock. With fully-onboard autonomy, MorphQuad demonstrates multi-revolution rotation while translating or hovering, for pipe inspection and target tracking (maneuverability); valve turning, perching, and object pressing and pushing with human-level strengths (manipulation); and wind rejection from any direction, even directed to a single rotor, and push-pull recovery (resiliency).

</details>


### [4] [Metallic Ultrasound Waveguides as a Distributed Tactile Sensing Platform for Contact Localization, Force Estimation, and Material Class Discrimination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02827)
*Alexandros Rosakis,Alessio Tamborini,Basile Fakhoury,Cole Bailey,Morteza Gharib*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文研究了金属超声波导作为分布式触觉传感器的可行性，通过单一近端换能器即可实现大面积、多点接触的定位、力估计和接触材料分类，突破了传统触觉传感器在面积与复杂度之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人触觉传感方案在传感面积与系统复杂度之间存在权衡：大面积通常意味着传感器单元数量激增、布线复杂。作者旨在探索一种利用金属超声波导实现分布式触觉感知的新途径，仅需单一换能器即可覆盖大面积并实现多点检测。

Method: 以金属超声波导为载体，在近端安装单一换能器发射和接收超声波。通过圆柱压头施加单点和双点接触，记录波导的反射与透射系数。分析反射/透射比(R/T)与接触力的线性关系，利用反射能量分配作为与力无关的材料特征参数进行材料分类，并将该方法从一维波导扩展至二维金属板以验证接触定位能力。

Result: 单点接触下，力与R/T呈线性关系（9种材料R²≥0.95），校准斜率与材料有效接触模量呈强对数相关（Pearson r=-0.98）；反射能量分配比可作为力无关参数实现材料分类。双压头实验中，两处接触力均可从波导信号中恢复，与力传感器测量高度吻合（接触点1 R²=0.97，接触点2 R²=0.95）。二维金属板实验确认了接触定位和材料相关效应。

Conclusion: 金属波导是一种稳健的分布式触觉传感平台，能够同时实现接触定位、力估计和接触材料分类，为机器人触觉感知提供了一种面积大、复杂度低的解决方案。

Abstract: Tactile sensing is central to how robotic systems interact with the real world, yet current solutions face a tradeoff between sensing area and system complexity. This work investigates metallic ultrasound waveguides as distributed tactile sensors fully interrogated from a single proximal transducer. Using cylindrical indenters, we characterized the acoustic response to single and multi-point contacts with varying forces and contact materials. For single point indentation, the applied force was well captured by a linear relationship with the ratio of the reflection to transmission coefficients (F = a * R/T) across all nine tested materials (R2 >= 0.95). The calibration slope, a, correlated strongly with the material's effective contact modulus (log--log Pearson r=-0.98). The reflected energy partition was found to be a load-independent parameter related to the contacting material's properties, enabling material classification independent of force. For the two-indenter experiment, both contact forces were recovered from the waveguide signal and were in close agreement with reference load cell measurements (contact 1, R2 = 0.97; contact 2, R2=0.95). The approach was extended to two-dimensional metallic sheets, confirming both contact localization and material-dependent effects. Overall, these results validate metallic waveguides as a robust platform for distributed tactile sensing, providing contact localization, force estimation, and material-class discrimination for the contacting body.

</details>


### [5] [TACO: TActile World Model as a Self-COrrector forScalable VLA Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02840)
*Shengbang Liu,Yueru Jia,Yuyang Yan,Jiaming Liu,Xinran Zhang,Qiuxuan Feng,Yandong Guo,Shiji Zhou,Boxin Shi,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: TACO 是一个触觉感知的世界模型驱动框架，通过"识别-想象-标注"循环将真实世界失败转化为想象的视觉-触觉修正，用于 VLA 模型在接触密集操作任务中的可扩展后训练，实现了 44% 的绝对成功率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA 模型在接触密集的机器人操作任务中容易因微小接触扰动而产生不可恢复的局部失败，这类失败难以仅靠视觉检测。通过触觉感知的修正性后训练可以改善恢复能力，但依赖人工干预扩展监督成本过高；而纯视觉世界模型可能生成视觉上合理但接触不一致的轨迹，无法可靠地提供触觉层面的修正监督。

Method: TACO 框架包含三个核心组件：(1) Recognize-Imagine-Label 循环：统一的 progress-action 模型利用进度估计识别失败邻近状态，视觉-触觉生成模型想象局部修正片段，progress-action 模型为其标注可执行修正动作；(2) 知识隔离的触觉适应（knowledge-insulated tactile adaptation）：在微调 VLA 时保护预训练的视觉-语言先验不被破坏；(3) 优势条件训练（advantage-conditioned training）：使策略能够从想象的修正中学习。整个流程将真实世界的失败转化为想象的视觉-触觉修正，用于迭代式 VLA 后训练。

Result: 在真实世界的接触密集操作任务上，TACO 相比基础策略实现了 44% 的绝对成功率提升，相比未使用知识隔离触觉适应的策略提升了 32%。

Conclusion: TACO 通过将触觉感知的世界模型引入 VLA 后训练流程，有效解决了接触密集任务中的局部失败恢复问题，且通过知识隔离策略保护了预训练先验，为可扩展的机器人操作策略改进提供了新路径。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown promising generalization in robotic manipulation, but they still struggle with contact-rich tasks, where minor contact perturbations can cause unrecoverable failures that are hard to detect from vision alone. Since these failures are localized rather than task-level semantic errors, tactile-aware corrective post-training offers an efficient way to improve recovery. However, scaling such supervision through human intervention is costly. Recent works have explored world models to synthesize imagined rollouts for policy improvement, but vision-only world models may produce visually plausible yet contact-inconsistent trajectories. We therefore introduce TACO, a tactile-aware world-model-driven framework for scalable VLA post-training in contact-rich manipulation. Given real robot rollouts, TACO follows a Recognize-Imagine-Label loop with a tactile-aware world model: a unified progress-action model recognizes failure-adjacent states using progress estimates, a visuo-tactile generation model imagines local correction segments, and the progress-action model labels them with executable corrective actions. To incorporate tactile corrective supervision into VLA post-training, TACO combines knowledge-insulated tactile adaptation with advantage-conditioned training, enabling the policy to learn from imagined corrections without degrading pretrained visual-language priors. These components enable TACO to convert real-world failures into imagined visuo-tactile corrections for iterative VLA post-training. Experiments on real-world contact-rich manipulation tasks show that TACO achieves 44% absolute success rate improvement over the base policy and 32% over the policy without knowledge-insulated tactile adaptation.

</details>


### [6] [CLEAR: Closed-Loop Reinforcement Learning at Scale for End-to-End Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02841)
*Yunxiao Shi,Hong Cai,Mohammad Ghavamzadeh,Fatih Porikli*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CLEAR 提出了一种面向端到端自动驾驶的闭环强化学习训练系统，通过残差航点策略（residual waypoint policy）和异构分布式训练流水线，在 CARLA longest6 v2 和 Bench2Drive 上取得了最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 VLA（视觉-语言-动作）自动驾驶策略主要依赖模仿学习，在开环训练与闭环推理之间存在分布偏移（distribution shift），导致闭环规划性能欠佳。亟需一种能够规模化进行闭环强化学习训练的方法来弥补这一差距。

Method: (1) 提出残差航点策略（residual waypoint policy）：在预训练 VLA 策略的航点先验（waypoint prior）基础上学习残差，有效利用预训练知识；(2) 设计异构流水线（heterogeneous pipeline）：将仿真器和 VLA 学习器部署在不同计算集群上，大幅增加并行仿真环境数量，避免资源争用并保持训练稳定性；(3) 使用简洁的奖励函数进行强化学习训练。

Result: CLEAR 显著超越此前方法，在 CARLA longest6 v2 和 Bench2Drive 两个具有挑战性的基准上取得了新的 state-of-the-art 性能。

Conclusion: 通过闭环强化学习训练结合残差策略与异构分布式架构，CLEAR 有效解决了 VLA 策略中开环到闭环的分布偏移问题，为端到端自动驾驶的 RL 规模化训练提供了可行方案。

Abstract: End-to-end autonomous driving (E2E-AD) aims to directly map raw sensor information to driving actions. Recently, with the rapid advancement of multi-modal large language models (MLLMs), researchers have proposed the paradigm of Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models for E2E-AD, where it seeks to integrate visual perception, language understanding and action prediction within a single policy. However, existing VLA-based policies largely adopts imitation learning, where it only learns to drive by optimizing distance-based metrics w.r.t. logged expert trajectories. Such distribution shift between open-loop training and closed-loop inference leads to suboptimal performance in closed-loop planning. To close this gap, we present CLEAR, a system that enables closed-loop training using Reinforcement Learning (RL) at scale for E2E-AD. We propose to learn a novel residual waypoint policy around the waypoint prior from pretrained VLA policies, effectively harnessing the knowledge within. On another front, one of the key challenges to scale up RL for vision-based policies is the number of parallel simulation environments since RL is data hungry. To that end, we design a heterogeneous pipeline that places the simulator and the VLA learner on distinct compute groups, which allows us to dramatically increase the number of simulation environments running in parallel while avoiding resource contention and maintaining training stability. We show that with a simple reward, CLEAR significantly outperforms previous methods and sets new state-of-the-art performance on the challenging benchmarks of CARLA longest6 v2 and Bench2Drive.

</details>


### [7] [Differential Amplifier-Inspired AmpAttention for Multi-View Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02845)
*Jin Yang,Ping Wei,Nanning Zheng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出受模拟电路中差分放大器启发的AmpAttention注意力机制，用于抑制多视图机器人操控中的注意力漂移。基于此构建RVAF模型，在18项RLBench任务上取得最优平均成功率，训练时间缩短33.3%，并在真实世界高精度任务中验证有效性；扩展版RVAF++结合SAM2图像编码器，在"插销"任务上达到91%成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多视图机器人操控方法虽借助注意力机制取得进展，但机器人视角图像固有的冗余性、遮挡和视角依赖性导致了严重的"注意力漂移"（attention drift）问题，影响感知可靠性，亟需一种能够抑制噪声、提取高信噪比信号的注意力机制。

Method: 1. 提出AmpAttention注意力机制，灵感来源于模拟电路中的差分放大器，旨在抑制注意力噪声、捕捉高信噪比信号；2. 构建RVAF模型，融合任务引导的视角内（intra-view）和视角间（inter-view）AmpAttention；3. 进一步扩展为RVAF++，整合SAM2图像编码器以增强高精度任务表现。

Result: 1. RVAF在18项RLBench任务（249个变体）上取得最优平均成功率，且训练时间比先前SOTA方法减少33.3%；2. 在真实世界高精度任务（如拾取飞镖并精准插入红色靶心）中展现强潜力；3. RVAF++在"insert peg"任务上达到91%成功率。

Conclusion: AmpAttention有效解决了多视图机器人操控中的注意力漂移问题，RVAF及其扩展版本在仿真和真实世界任务中均表现出色，兼顾了训练效率和任务精度，尤其在高精度操控任务上具有显著优势。

Abstract: Multi-view robotic manipulation methods with the attention mechanism have recently achieved significant progress in both training efficiency and task performance. However, the inherent redundancy, occlusion, and viewpoint dependency in robotic view images often lead to severe attention drift. To address this challenge, we propose AmpAttention, a novel attention mechanism inspired by differential amplifiers in analog circuits. It aims to suppress attention noise and capture high signal-to-noise ratio signals for more reliable perception. Based on this, we introduce the RVAF model, which integrates task-guided intra-view and inter-view AmpAttention. Compared to previous state-of-the-art methods, RVAF achieves the optimal average success rate across 18 RLBench tasks (249 variations) while reducing training time by 33.3\%. RVAF also demonstrates strong potential in real-world high-precision tasks, exemplified by its ability to pick up a dart and accurately insert it into the red bullseye. Furthermore, we extend RVAF to RVAF++ by incorporating the SAM2 image encoder. RVAF++ achieves substantial gains on high-precision tasks, achieving a 91\% success rate on the `insert peg' task. More qualitative results are provided at the anonymous project website https://anonymous.4open.science/w/RVAF-Anonymization.

</details>


### [8] [DREAMSTEER: Latent World Models Can Steer VLA Policies During Deployment Without Any Finetuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02865)
*Hanchen Cui,Sergio Arnaud,Arjun Majumdar,Daniel Dugas,Elie Aljalbout,Karthik Desingh,Krishna Murthy Jatavallabhula,Franziska Meier*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: DREAMSTEER 是一种无需微调的部署期引导框架，通过潜在世界模型和价值模型对预训练 VLA 策略生成的候选动作进行想象与排序，显著提升了真实场景下的任务成功率和指令遵循准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略在部署时面临分布偏移，导致鲁棒性下降和指令遵循不一致。现有方法依赖目标环境中的演示数据进行微调，但在许多部署场景中难以获取此类数据。

Method: 提出 DREAMSTEER 框架：(1) 从 VLA 策略和预定义运动基元中采样候选动作块；(2) 使用动作条件化的潜在世界模型想象各候选动作的执行结果；(3) 通过语言条件化的价值模型对想象轨迹进行排序，选择最优动作执行。整个过程无需微调或修改模型参数。

Result: 在四个包含未见物体的真实世界操作基准测试中，DREAMSTEER 将任务成功率从基础 VLA 策略的 23.75% 提升至 66.25%，指令遵循准确率从 38.75% 提升至 56.25%。

Conclusion: DREAMSTEER 证明了利用潜在世界模型和价值模型在部署时引导预训练 VLA 策略是可行且有效的，为无需微调的鲁棒机器人操作提供了新思路。

Abstract: Pretrained vision-language-action (VLA) policies show promising zero-shot generalization, but often fail under deployment-time distribution shift, leading to decreased robustness and inconsistent instruction following. While prior work commonly tackles this by finetuning on in-distribution data, it assumes demonstrations collected on tasks in the target environment. In this work, we propose DREAMSTEER, a deployment-time steering framework for pretrained VLAs without any finetuning or parameter modifications. The key insight in DREAMSTEER is to leverage a latent world model and a value model to steer pretrained VLA policies. During deployment, DREAMSTEER samples candidate action chunks from a VLA policy and predefined motion primitives, imagines their outcomes using an action-conditioned latent world model, and ranks the imagined trajectories with a language-conditioned value model. Across four real-world manipulation benchmarks with unseen objects, DREAMSTEER improves task success rate from 23.75% to 66.25% and instruction-following accuracy from 38.75% to 56.25% over the base VLA policy.

### [9] [Continuous-Time Gaussian Belief Trees for Motion Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02884)
*Rayan Mazouz,Qi Heng Ho,Zachary N. Sunberg,Morteza Lahijanian*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种面向连续时间随机系统的采样信念规划框架，结合连续时间信念传播与信念障碍函数安全验证，解决传统离散时间方法遗漏采样间约束违反的问题，在狭窄通道等场景中实现高成功率和概率安全保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统采样运动规划方法通常采用离散时间节点检查安全约束，无法检测连续轨迹上相邻采样点之间发生的概率约束违反，在过程噪声和测量噪声同时存在的情况下，这种遗漏会导致严重的安全隐患。

Method: 1) 将机器人动力学建模为连续时间线性随机微分方程，传感器测量在离散时刻到达；2) 推导离线混合信念传播模型：信念在测量之间按连续时间ODE演化，在测量时刻执行离散Kalman滤波更新跳变；3) 引入基于信念障碍函数的安全检验器，实现段级别（segment-level）的概率安全验证，覆盖整段连续轨迹；4) 将该框架与RRT和SST规划器集成。

Result: 在多个基准环境中评估，所提方法取得了高成功率，且能够稳健地执行机会约束；在狭窄通道场景中，离散时间对照方法因遗漏采样间不安全行为而失败，而本方法成功完成任务。

Conclusion: 该框架为连续时间随机系统下的采样信念规划提供了原则性解决方案，将连续时间不确定性传播与连续时间安全要求统一建模，有效弥补了传统节点检查方法的固有缺陷。

Abstract: We address sampling-based motion planning for continuous-time stochastic systems under process and measurement uncertainty, with probabilistic guarantees on safety and performance. The robot dynamics are modeled as a continuous-time linear stochastic differential equation, while sensor measurements arrive at discrete time instants. We derive an offline hybrid belief propagation model in which the belief evolves according to continuous-time ODEs between measurements and undergoes discrete Kalman filter update jumps at measurement times. To ensure safety, we introduce a belief-barrier-function-based safety checker for segment-level probabilistic verification. This enables the planner to certify safety over entire continuous trajectory segments and detect inter-sample chance-constraint violations that are missed by conventional node-based checks. Together, these components provide a principled framework for sampling-based belief planning that accounts for both continuous-time uncertainty propagation and continuous-time safety requirements. We integrate the method with RRT and SST planners and evaluate it across multiple benchmark environments. The results show that the proposed method achieves high success rates and robust enforcement of chance constraints, including in narrow-passage scenarios where discrete-time counterparts fail due to missed inter-sample unsafe behavior.

### [10] [Longitudinal-Motion-Aware Lateral Control for Autonomous Vehicles: A Robust Nonlinear Control Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02924)
*Sixu Li,Nitesh Kumar,Reyshwanth Ganeshan,Sivakumar Rathinam,Swaroop Darbha,Yang Zhou*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动驾驶横向控制器多假设恒定速度或固定工作点，且在瞬态纵向机动时性能退化；同时多数方法假设车辆参数精确已知，难以应对实际参数不确定性。

Method: 首先推导依赖纵向速度和加速度的跟踪误差模型；采用反馈线性化获得线性输入输出关系，将纵向运动嵌入控制律，并分析内部动力学稳定性；进而提出两种鲁棒设计：(i) 受滑模控制启发的Lyapunov重设计方法，(ii) 增量非线性动态逆(INDI)方法，均证明最终有界性并明确鲁棒调参参数。

Result: 仿真表明在不同速度和加速度下跟踪精度提升、性能一致性好且对模型不确定性具有鲁棒性；实车测试验证了实时可实现性和实际路径跟踪性能。

Conclusion: 该框架有效解决了变纵向运动条件下的横向控制问题，两种鲁棒方案各有实现权衡，均为参数不确定下的自动驾驶横向控制提供了可行解。

Abstract: As autonomous vehicles (AVs) operate in increasingly dynamic traffic conditions, lateral control must be performed while longitudinal speed and acceleration vary. Yet many existing lateral controllers rely on constant-speed or operating-point-based assumptions, which can degrade performance during transient longitudinal maneuvers. Moreover, most methods assume precisely known vehicle parameters, despite real-world parametric uncertainties. To address these limitations, this paper presents a longitudinal-motion-aware robust nonlinear lateral control framework for AVs. It first derives a tracking error model that depends on varying longitudinal speed and acceleration. Using this model, feedback linearization is employed to obtain a linear input-output relation for lateral error tracking while embedding longitudinal motion into the control law. The resulting internal dynamics are then analyzed to ensure overall system stability. To address parameter uncertainty, two robust control designs with distinct implementation trade-offs are proposed: (i) a Lyapunov redesign (LR) approach inspired by sliding mode control, and (ii) an incremental nonlinear dynamic inversion (INDI) method. Both are rigorously analyzed and proven to ensure ultimate boundedness, with key robustness-tuning parameters explicitly identified. Simulations demonstrate enhanced tracking accuracy, consistent performance across varying speeds and accelerations, and robustness to model uncertainties, while also examining the effects of the robustness-related parameters. Real-vehicle tests further confirm real-time implementation and practical path-tracking performance on actual hardware.

### [11] [Function-Space Diffusion for Motion Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02977)
*Zinuo Chang,Yipu Chen,Byoungwoo Park,Hongzhe Yu,Yongxin Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: FSD-MP 将运动规划中的轨迹建模为连续函数，在函数空间（谱域）中直接进行扩散，使用 Matérn 协方差驱动的高斯噪声定义模态前向过程，并用离散正弦变换傅里叶神经算子（DST-FNO）参数化反向过程，实现了离散化不变的轨迹生成，可在训练分辨率上零样本泛化至最高 16 倍分辨率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散的运动规划器通常对固定长度的路径点序列进行操作，导致学习到的模型依赖分辨率，无法在不同分辨率之间实现零样本泛化。作者希望实现一种离散化不变的轨迹生成方法，使模型在一次训练后可泛化到任意分辨率。

Method: 提出 Function-Space Diffusion for Motion Planning (FSD-MP)。核心思路：1）将轨迹建模为连续函数，在函数空间而非离散序列上进行扩散；2）定义谱域中的模态前向过程，噪声由 Matérn 型协方差的高斯过程驱动；3）反向过程使用基于离散正弦变换的傅里叶神经算子（DST-FNO）参数化，该算子天然兼容边界条件，可在不同分辨率下保持起点-目标约束；4）在 2D 点机器人和 7-DoF Franka 机械臂基准上进行评估。

Result: FSD-MP 在训练分辨率下达到了有竞争力的规划性能，并且能够在高达 16 倍于训练分辨率的情况下实现零样本泛化，无需重新训练即可保持一致的规划行为。

Conclusion: 函数空间扩散为离散化不变的运动规划提供了一个有效的框架，打破了传统扩散规划器分辨率依赖的限制，展示了跨分辨率泛化的能力。

Abstract: Diffusion-based motion planners have demonstrated strong performance in generating diverse and high-quality robot trajectories in cluttered environments with multiple feasible solutions. However, existing approaches typically operate on fixed-length waypoint sequences, making the learned model resolution-dependent, thereby preventing zero-shot generalization across resolutions. In this work, we propose Function-Space Diffusion for Motion Planning (FSD-MP), a diffusion-based motion planner that models trajectories as continuous functions and performs diffusion directly in function space, achieving discretization-invariant trajectory generation. We define a mode-wise forward process in the spectral domain, driven by Gaussian noise with a Matérn-type covariance, and parameterize the reverse process with a boundary-compatible Discrete Sine Transform-based Fourier Neural Operator (DST-FNO) that preserves start-goal constraints across resolutions. We evaluate FSD-MP on 2D point robot and 7-DoF Franka manipulator planning benchmarks. Our method achieves competitive planning performance at the training resolution and generalizes zero-shot across resolutions up to 16$\times$ higher, preserving consistent planning behavior without retraining. These results demonstrate that function-space diffusion provides an effective framework for discretization-invariant motion planning.

</details>


### [12] [Beyond Heuristics: A Standardized Real2Sim Pipeline for Physical Human Robot Interaction in Human-in-the-Loop Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03017)
*Chengyuan Yang,Yifan Wang,Chun Kwang Tan,Sherwin Stephen Chan,Youlong Wang,Xiaoyue Yan,Lei Li,Wei Tech Ang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种Real2Sim流程，通过CMA-ES进化策略从用户"安全舒适"反馈中辨识骨盆-绑带界面的6自由度粘弹性参数，实现人机物理交互的精确建模，支持人因数字孪生的高保真仿真。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 老龄化社会推动辅助机器人需求增长，但物理测试的安全风险和成本高昂。人在回路仿真虽具吸引力，其耦合系统的保真度受限于交互模型参数多采用启发式整定而非数据辨识，尤其绑带松紧度在不同人体测量参数间存在模糊性，缺乏可复现的标定方法。

Method: 将骨盆-绑带界面建模为6自由度粘弹性机制（12个方向刚度和阻尼参数）。采用CMA-ES进化策略，以用户"安全舒适"主观反馈作为可复现操作点，逐受试者辨识参数。通过五名受试者的组内相关系数分析，区分共享参数与个体特异性参数，构建先验参数集。对新受试者仅需精调12个参数中的5个即可完成标定。将标定模型部署至人因数字孪生中验证步态适应效果。

Result: 标定模型成功复现真实交互包络，并在人因数字孪生中诱导出生物力学上准确的步态适应。过软和过硬的极端设置均失效，证实存在一个正确的操作点，且启发式整定无法可靠选择该点。先验参数配置使新受试者标定仅需调整5/12的参数。

Conclusion: 该Real2Sim流程提升了人在回路仿真的保真度，证明人因数字孪生可作为个性化控制器临床前验证的预测工具，避免了启发式整定的不可靠性。

Abstract: The aging global population drives demand for assistive robots, yet the safety risks and costs of physical testing make Human-in-the-Loop (HITL) simulation an attractive alternative. Its fidelity for coupled systems, however, is limited by interaction models whose impedance parameters are tuned heuristically rather than identified from data. We present a Real2Sim pipeline that identifies the coupled Physical Human-Robot Interaction (pHRI) dynamics of a pelvis--strap interface on an overground mobile balance assistant. The interface is modeled as a 6-DoF viscoelastic mechanism whose 12 directional stiffness and damping parameters are identified per subject via Covariance Matrix Adaptation Evolution Strategy (CMA-ES), using the user's ``Safe \& Comfortable'' feedback as a reproducible operating point that resolves harness-tightness ambiguity across anthropometrics. An intraclass-correlation analysis over a five-subject cohort separates shareable from subject-specific parameters, yielding a set of prior parameters derived from the existing data. Deploying this prior configures a previously unseen subject by refining only 5 of the 12 parameters. The calibrated model then reproduces the real interaction envelope and induces biomechanically accurate gait adaptations in the Human Digital Twin (HDT). Overly compliant and overly stiff settings, by contrast, fail as extreme settings, confirming a correct operating point that no heuristic tuning procedure can reliably select. The pipeline thus improves HITL simulation fidelity and supports the Human Digital Twin as a predictive tool for pre-clinical verification of personalized controllers.

This paper presents the Dynamic Robotic Balance Assistant (DRBA), a novel gait trainer providing assist-as-needed body weight and balance support for various training scenarios. DRBA integrates a 3-degree-of-freedom (3-DoF) robotic arm for pelvic support with flexible motion, a compact sit-to-stand assistance module, and user-following and fall detection algorithms to ensure minimal interference and responsive support. Experimental results demonstrated high transparency, with minimal impact on natural gait dynamics. A patient trial with nine elderly patients with varying medical conditions and balance impairments (ranging from severe to mild) further validated DRBA's effectiveness. The results showed that DRBA-assisted training increased step length and walking speed compared to therapist-assisted gait training. Additionally, DRBA enabled users to perform tasks beyond their unaided ability, expanding rehabilitation possibilities. These findings highlight DRBA's potential to enhance rehabilitation outcomes by facilitating higher training intensity and enabling task-oriented exercises.

### [14] [Exp2VLA: Enabling Vision-Language-Action for Drone Navigation from Expert Demonstrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03146)

Method: 提出专家蒸馏流水线（Exp2VLA）：首先从强化学习、遥操作或其他控制器获取专家行为，将其转化为训练数据，随后用这些数据对紧凑型VLA模型进行微调，从而将不同来源的控制策略统一到语言条件导航模型中，降低手工集成成本。

In this work, we propose a practical expert-distillation pipeline (Exp2VLA) for language-conditioned drone navigation. This allows existing control strategies to be transferred into a unified language-guided navigation model, reducing manual system integration and lowering the barrier for deploying new robot behaviors. Experiments in both sim-to-sim and simulation-in-the-loop settings across multi-object scenes show that the fine-tuned models can handle varied semantic commands and generalize to unseen target compositions. ### [15] [Hope for the Best, Prepare for the Worst: Occlusion-Aware Contingency Planning for Autonomous Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03155)

Building on our previous methods that apply reachability analysis to sequentially determine the possible states of hidden traffic participants, we integrate a tree-based motion planner capable of reasoning over future observations and the absence thereof. ### [16] [Beyond Point-Attached Semantics: Object-Centric Semantic Fields for Generalizable Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03163)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（原始点云、2D特征提升、离散3D逐点特征）的语义信息都依附于观测相关的采样点，随视角、传感器配置和物体实例变化，缺乏稳定、显式的3D功能部件语义，制约了机器人操作的泛化能力。

Method: 提出一种以物体为中心的连续语义场（object-centric continuous semantic field），以物体点云为条件，在任意显式3D查询位置输出部件感知语义嵌入。该场从部件标注的物体模型训练，训练后冻结，用于生成语义点云作为操作策略的物体级条件输入。

Result: 在RoboTwin仿真任务和真实世界双臂物体操作实验中，该方法比原始点云、2D特征提升和3D逐点特征基线提供更稳定的功能部件线索，并提升了策略性能。

Conclusion: 以物体为中心的连续语义场通过解耦语义与观测采样点，提供了更稳定、泛化的功能部件表征，显著提升了机器人操作策略的性能，验证了其在仿真和真实场景中的有效性。

Abstract: Generalizable robot manipulation requires stable 3D understanding of functional object parts, such as handles, tool heads, openings, and graspable regions. Raw point clouds provide geometry but lack explicit part semantics, and their sampled points vary with viewpoint, sensor configuration, and object instance. Existing 2D feature lifting and discrete 3D point-wise features enrich point clouds with semantics, but the resulting features remain attached to observation-dependent samples. We propose an object-centric continuous semantic field that conditions on an object point cloud and reads part-aware semantic embeddings at explicit 3D query locations. The field is trained from part-annotated object models and then frozen to generate semantic point clouds as object-level conditioning for manipulation policies. Experiments on RoboTwin simulation tasks and real-world bimanual object manipulation show that our representation provides more stable functional-part cues and improves policy performance over raw point-cloud, 2D feature lifting, and 3D point-wise feature baselines. Project Page: \href{https://zainzh.github.io/beyond-point-attached-semantics}{https://zainzh.github.io/beyond-point-attached-semantics}.

### [17] [AnchorVLA: Bridging Discrete Decisions and Continuous Trajectories for Vision-Language-Action Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03182)
*Qi Liu,Yabei Li,Hongsong Wang,Heng Zhang,Lei He*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: AnchorVLA提出了一种层次化的决策锚定VLA规划框架，使用轨迹模式锚点作为高层VLA推理与连续轨迹执行之间的显式接口，解决了现有VLA规划器中语义-动作对齐困难、离散化误差和推理效率低的问题，在Bench2Drive闭环基准上取得SOTA成功率77.28。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA规划器主要分为两类：基于规划头的轨迹预测（VLA推理对连续轨迹生成的约束较弱）和全轨迹自回归生成（依赖低信息密度的坐标token序列，语义-动作对齐困难，存在离散化误差且推理效率低下）。因此需要一种既能充分利用VLA推理能力又能高效生成高质量连续轨迹的新框架。

Method: 提出AnchorVLA框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) Decision-as-Anchor Representation：将行为级驾驶决策编码为锚点token，每个锚点编码完整的局部运动模式而非单一坐标点；(2) Decision-Anchored Residual Flow：在选定锚点定义的残差空间中生成细粒度连续轨迹，捕获高层决策后的多模态执行细化。

Result: 在Bench2Drive闭环基准上，AnchorVLA取得了77.28的SOTA成功率（Success Rate）和89.92的竞争性驾驶分数（Driving Score）。

Conclusion: 通过在紧凑且语义有意义的锚点上进行推理而非自回归生成航点序列，AnchorVLA在保持LLM决策能力的同时，提升了推理效率、语义-动作对齐和连续生成的灵活性，为VLA自动驾驶规划提供了一种有效的层次化解决方案。

Abstract: Autonomous driving planning requires translating navigation intent, traffic rules, dynamic interactions, and language instructions into executable continuous trajectories. Vision-Language-Action models have been introduced into driving planning to improve long-tail generalization, commonsense reasoning, high-level semantic understanding, and explainability. However, existing VLA planners mainly follow planning-head-based trajectory prediction or full-trajectory autoregressive generation. The former only weakly constrains continuous trajectory generation with VLA reasoning, while the latter relies on long sequences of low-information-density coordinate tokens, making semantic-action alignment difficult and leading to discretization errors and inefficient inference. To address these limitations, we propose AnchorVLA, a hierarchical decision-anchored VLA planning framework that uses trajectory-pattern anchors as an explicit interface between high-level VLA reasoning and continuous trajectory execution. Specifically, Decision-as-Anchor Representation represents behavior-level driving decisions with anchor tokens, each encoding an entire local motion pattern rather than a single coordinate point. Decision-Anchored Residual Flow then generates fine-grained continuous trajectories in the selected anchor-defined residual space, capturing multi-modal execution refinements after high-level decision making. By reasoning over compact and semantically meaningful anchors instead of autoregressively generating waypoint sequences, AnchorVLA preserves LLM-based decision making while improving inference efficiency, semantic-action alignment, and continuous generation flexibility. Experiments on the Bench2Drive closed-loop benchmark show that AnchorVLA achieves a state-of-the-art Success Rate of 77.28 and a competitive Driving Score of 89.92.

</details>

*Yuya Hamamatsu,Maarja Kruusmaa,Asko Ristolainen*

TL;DR: 提出一种基于GNN+Transformer+MDN的布局无关控制分配器，结合可微分物理代理模型实现推理时指令优化，可在不同执行器布局间零样本部署，仿真和真实水池实验均验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统控制分配器高度依赖于特定的执行器几何布局，更换布局需重新设计或调参，缺乏通用性。因此需要一种能在不同执行器配置间零样本泛化的控制分配方法。

Method: 1) 使用图神经网络(GNN)和Transformer将机器人几何布局建模为图结构；2) 混合密度网络(MDN)预测多模态控制指令分布；3) 可微分物理代理模型用于推理阶段指令优化，以最小化目标力/力矩跟踪误差和能耗；4) 使用随机生成的执行器布局数据进行单一广义模型训练。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了控制分配器对执行器布局的零样本泛化，结合推理时优化可在未知布局上达到与传统布局专用控制器相当的性能，具有显著的工程应用潜力。

Abstract: In this study, we propose a layout-independent control allocator capable of zero-shot deployment across diverse actuator configurations. The proposed method utilizes a learning pipeline that integrates a Graph Neural Network (GNN) and a Transformer to represent the robot's geometric layout as a graph, along with a Mixture Density Network (MDN) to predict multi-modal control command distributions. Furthermore, by incorporating a differentiable physics surrogate model, we achieve command refinement during inference to minimize target wrench tracking error and energy consumption. A single generalized model using randomly generated actuator layout data demonstrated high trajectory tracking performance on different actuator layout robots outside the training distribution. Additionally, in real-world pool experiments, our approach achieved performance nearly equivalent to conventional controllers designed to specific layouts.

### [19] [Derivations of Error-State Kalman Filter Kinematics for Globally Applicable Aided Inertial Navigation Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03211)
*Antonia Hager,Torleiv H. Bryne*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文系统性地给出了四种适用于全球辅助惯性导航系统的经典与不变性误差状态卡尔曼滤波器（ESKF）的数学公式，包括标准滤波器、左不变滤波器和右不变滤波器，旨在为比较和实现提供参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全球导航系统需处理地球曲率、自转和重力变化等因素，而这些在局部导航中常被忽略。经典ESKF的误差状态动力学依赖于轨迹，而不变性ESKF利用李群对称性可使群仿射系统的误差传播与轨迹无关。然而，在标准滤波器、左不变滤波器和右不变滤波器之间做出选择取决于系统动力学和传感器配置，目前缺乏一个系统性的数学公式参考。

Method: 本文以数学笔记的形式，详细推导并整理了四种ESKF的完整公式：标准ESKF（位置和速度误差在导航坐标系中加性定义）、左不变ESKF（误差在体坐标系中表示）和右不变ESKF（误差在导航/世界坐标系中表示），涵盖全球适用的辅助惯性导航系统场景。

Result: 提供了一套统一、系统的数学公式框架，清晰对比了四种滤波器的误差状态定义、传播模型和更新方程，为工程实现和滤波器选型提供了直接参考。

Conclusion: 本文作为系统性参考笔记，填补了全球导航应用中多种ESKF公式缺乏统一整理的空白，有助于研究者和工程师根据具体系统动力学和传感器配置选择合适的滤波器结构。

Abstract: Global navigation systems require state estimation algorithms that handle Earth's curvature, Earth's rotation, and gravitational variations. These factors can typically be neglected in local navigation algorithms for robots, drones, etc. In classical error-state Kalman Filtering (ESKF) the error state dynamics are trajectory-dependent. Invariant ESKFs utilize Lie Group symmetries to represent the error, which can render error propagation trajectory-independent for group-affine systems. Choosing between a standard filter (where position and velocity errors are defined additively in the navigation frame), a left-invariant filter (where errors are represented in the body frame) and a right-invariant filter (where errors are represented in the navigation/world frame) depends on system dynamics and sensor configuration. This note presents the mathematical formulas for four classical and invariant ESKFs for globally applicable aided inertial navigation systems. It is intended to serve as a systematic reference for comparison and implementation.

</details>


### [20] [Strouhal-Aware Model Predictive Control for Efficient Multi-Fin Flapping Locomotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03216)
*Yuya Hamamatsu,Zixi Chen,Maarja Kruusmaa,Asko Ristolainen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该文将生物启发的Strouhal数最优窗口原则嵌入模型预测控制(MPC)，在四软鳍自主水下航行器上实现实时调控，使巡航功耗降低8.8%–32%，并将最大航速从0.3 m/s提升至0.4 m/s。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界中高效扑动推进依赖于狭窄的Strouhal数窗口以获得最大推功比，但这一经验法则尚未被转化为水下机器人的实时控制策略。现有方法缺乏对流动物理第一性原理的显式约束，导致能量效率受限、高速巡航不可达。

Method: 提出Strouhal感知的模型预测控制(MPC)：在准稳态水动力学模型的基础上，显式引入Strouhal偏离惩罚项，将问题构造为非凸优化；通过两阶段采样与梯度优化方法在嵌入式平台上以25 Hz实时求解。

Result: 水池与野外试验表明：(1)各鳍始终维持在最优Strouhal区间(0.25–0.35)；(2)在0.1–0.3 m/s巡航范围内，机械功率平均降低8.8%–32%；(3)实现0.4 m/s航速，而传统逆模型基线方法无法达到该速度。

Conclusion: 将第一性原理流动物理嵌入MPC目标函数，可在不牺牲敏捷性的前提下显著提升续航能力，为下一代多鳍机器人的能量感知运动控制提供了通用路径。

Abstract: Efficient flapping propulsion hinges on operating within a narrow Strouhal number window, a principle nature has converged upon for maximum thrust-to-power ratio. We translate this bioinspired empirical rule into real-time control, demonstrating it on an autonomous underwater vehicle driven by four soft fins. The proposed Strouhal-aware Model Predictive Control (MPC) enhances a quasi-steady hydrodynamic model with an explicit penalty for Strouhal deviation, solving the resulting nonconvex problem via a two-stage sampling and gradient optimization that runs onboard at 25 Hz. Pool and field trials show that the controller keeps each fin within the optimal Strouhal corridor (0.25-0.35) while precisely tracking commanded forces. This results in a mean reduction in mechanical power of 8.8\% to 32\% throughout the cruising range of 0.1 to 0.3 m/s. The proposed method also allows for a velocity of 0.4 m/s, which is unattainable for a baseline of the conventional inverse model. The results confirm that embedding first-principle flow physics into an MPC objective yields tangible endurance gains without sacrificing agility, offering a generic pathway to energy-aware locomotion in next-generation multifin robots.

### [21] [GDPR-Aware Trajectory Sharing for ISAC-Assisted Robot Navigation: A Case Study on FID-Constrained Collision Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03254)
*Zexin Fang,Bin Han,Donglin Wang,Fengchen Pei,Hans D. Schotten*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Fisher信息密度（FID）约束的轨迹共享方案，用于机器人避碰场景。该方案在共享前根据局部信息量对感知估计进行扰动，实验表明其在隐私-效用权衡上严格优于固定误差扰动，且符合GDPR数据最小化和完整性要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通感一体化（ISAC）虽赋能智能无线基础设施，但其产生的细粒度个人轨迹数据引发了日益严峻的监管合规问题。GDPR第5(1)(c)条（数据最小化）和第5(1)(f)条（完整性保护）要求个人数据限于必要范围并防止未经授权的重建。现有固定误差扰动方法在隐私-效用权衡上表现不佳，亟需一种有原则的信息感知扰动方案来同时满足这两项法规要求。

Method: 提出Fisher信息密度（FID）约束的轨迹共享框架：在机器人避碰场景中，系统先对感知估计计算局部Fisher信息量，依此对轨迹数据进行自适应扰动——信息密度高处施加更强扰动以限制重建泄露，信息密度低处扰动相对较小——然后再共享给其他节点，从而在信息论层面控制隐私泄露。

Result: 在真实行人轨迹数据集上的实验表明，FID控制共享方案在隐私-效用权衡上严格优于固定误差扰动。在匹配的漏检冲突率下，FID方案的重建泄露量和持续暴露时长均持续更低，验证了信息感知扰动作为一项有原则的技术措施的有效性。

Conclusion: 信息感知扰动（FID约束共享）可作为一种有原则的技术措施，与GDPR数据最小化及完整性保护要求对齐，为ISAC系统在满足法规合规前提下实现高效传感与通信提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Integrated sensing and communication (ISAC) enables intelligent wireless infrastructure but raises growing regulatory concern as fine-grained personal trajectory histories become a byproduct of sensing. General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR) Articles 5(1)(c) and 5(1)(f) require that personal data be limited to what is necessary and protected through appropriate technical measures against unauthorised reconstruction. This paper addresses both requirements through a Fisher information density (FID)-constrained trajectory sharing scheme for robot collision avoidance, where sensing estimates are perturbed according to local information content before sharing. Experiments on real pedestrian traces show that FID-controlled sharing achieves a strictly better privacy-utility tradeoff than fixed-error perturbation: at matched missed-conflict rates, reconstruction leakage and sustained exposure lengths are consistently lower, establishing information-aware perturbation as a principled technical measure aligned with GDPR data minimisation and integrity requirements.

</details>

Abstract: When designing robots' nonverbal behaviors, many researchers have turned to arts-based insights, such as Disney's Animation Principles. Yet, while these principles bear key insights into the design of like-life characters, their application to robot design is inherently limited, in part because animation is not constrained by real-world physics, and in part because animation principles focus on low level animation mechanics and not high-level design considerations for physically embodied, interactive characters. In contrast, little attention has been paid to art forms like puppetry, despite their long history of exploring morphological, behavior, and interaction design of physically embodied, interactive characters. As such, in this work we leverage puppetry texts and practicing puppeteers' expert knowledge knowledge to derive a set of puppetry principles with key insights for robot design. As we show, these insights go beyond -- and uniquely complement -- the prior insights provided by theater, dance, and animation.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多旋翼无人机搭载的连续体机械臂虽能实现柔顺空中操作，但末端载荷和螺旋桨下洗流会显著放大机械臂的面外弯曲与扭转变形，严重降低末端执行器的位姿精度，现有镍钛合金骨架设计在此类扰动下刚度不足，亟需一种能有效抵抗面外变形的结构方案。

Method: 提出一种基于万向节的连续体机械臂设计：采用管状骨架，集成弹簧增强的万向节以提升扭转刚度和面外弯曲刚度，并内置一体化导管用于内部线缆走线和流体输送。在静风及峰值下洗流条件下，搭载不同载荷进行台架试验，与镍钛合金骨架连续体机械臂进行对比；同时通过飞行中的耦合扰动测试评估悬停稳定性，并在喷水采样、定点喷洒和物体搬运等任务中进行系统演示验证。

Result: 台架试验表明，该设计在所有工况下均表现出更优的抗面外变形能力。在峰值下洗流条件下，与镍钛骨架设计相比：偏航方向平均误差降低2.5-4倍，Y轴方向降低2-45倍，滚转方向最多降低5倍。飞行耦合扰动测试验证了在不同载荷和驱动速度下的悬停稳定性。

Conclusion: 所提出的万向节基连续体机械臂通过结构创新有效解决了空中操作中面外变形导致的末端精度问题，在抗扭转和抗弯曲性能上全面优于传统镍钛合金骨架方案，并在多种实际空中作业场景中验证了其可行性与稳定性。

Abstract: Continuum manipulators mounted on multi-rotor UAVs enable compliant aerial manipulation, but payloads and propeller downwash amplify out-of-plane bending and twisting that degrade end-effector pose accuracy. To address this problem, we present a universal-joint-based continuum manipulator designed to improve resistance to out-of-plane deformation during aerial manipulation. The proposed design uses a tubular backbone with spring-reinforced universal joints and an integrated conduit for internal routing and fluid delivery. We evaluate the design in still air and under peak propeller downwash across varying payloads, and benchmark it against a prior Nitinol-backbone CM. Bench tests show improved resistance to out-of-plane deformation across all conditions. Under peak downwash, the proposed design reduces mean error by 2.5-4x in yaw, 2-45x in y-axis, and up to 5x in roll compared to the NiTi-backbone design. We further analyze hover stability through in-flight coupled-disturbance tests over varying payloads and actuation speeds, and demonstrate the system in water sampling, spot spraying, and object transport.

### [24] [Closed-loop vs. Open-loop Kalman Filter Architectures in Airborne Aided Inertial Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03338)
*Antonia Hager,Torleiv H. Bryne*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了开环（前馈）与闭环（反馈）误差状态卡尔曼滤波器在惯性导航系统中的性能差异，使用从消费级到导航级的多种IMU进行仿真，揭示了高端IMU在开环滤波中的平滑信息融合优势与闭环架构长期稳定性之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前，闭环误差状态卡尔曼滤波器是现代辅助惯性导航研究的主流，而安全关键型航空应用则坚持使用开环架构以确保计算单元的运行独立性和故障隔离。然而，这一架构选择长期缺乏定量的性能评估，仅有定性的系统安全性论证。本文旨在填补这一空白，量化两种架构在不同IMU等级下的实际性能影响。

Method: 采用大地坐标下的标准惯性力学编排，结合直接位置辅助。通过仿真手段，使用从消费级到导航级的多种惯性传感器误差特性，对开环与闭环两种滤波架构进行系统的性能对比分析。

Result: 仿真结果表明，高端IMU使用开环滤波器时具有更平滑的信息融合表现；而闭环架构则展现出固有的长期稳定性优势。两种架构之间存在明显的性能权衡，具体取决于IMU的精度等级。

Conclusion: 惯性导航系统中开环与闭环滤波架构的选择不仅涉及系统安全性考量，更直接影响导航性能。实际应用中应根据IMU等级和应用场景综合权衡，高端IMU可受益于开环架构的平滑融合特性，而长期稳定性需求则更倾向于闭环方案。

Abstract: Closed-loop (or feedback) error-state Kalman filters with their relatives and offspring are the state-of-the-art in modern aided inertial navigation research. Estimated inertial navigation system (INS) errors are continually fed back to the INS to correct the nominal system state before subsequent predictions. Conversely, in safety-critical aeronautical applications, open-loop (or feedforward) systems are an undisputed standard, where the inertial mechanization is strictly decoupled to allow for operational independence and fault isolation of computing units. We assess the performance impacts of this architectural choice beyond qualitative system-safety justifications using a standard inertial mechanization in geodetic coordinates and direct position aiding. Simulations using a variety of inertial sensor error characteristics, ranging from consumer to navigation grade systems, showcase the trade-off between smooth information fusion for high-end IMUs using an open-loop filter and the inherent long-term stability of the closed-loop architecture.

### [25] [Feeling the Unexpected: ResTacVLA for Contact-Rich Manipulation via Residual Tactile Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03387)
*Pengwei Zhang,Bin Xie,Ce Hao,Xinpan Meng,Xinyu Guo,Fang Deng,Long Cheng,Tiancai Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: ResTacVLA 受预测编码理论启发，将触觉数据重新定义为残差触觉表征（视觉先验与物理感知之间的差异），通过VQ瓶颈离散化为潜在接触基元，并利用视觉先验的不确定性自适应门控触觉整合，从而解决VLA模型中的模态崩溃问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在VLA模型中集成触觉感知时，高带宽视觉特征往往会淹没稀疏的触觉信号，导致模态崩溃。现有方法直接使用原始触觉数据，未能有效解决这种带宽不匹配问题。

Method: 1) 将触觉数据重新表述为残差触觉表征，捕获视觉先验与物理感知之间的差异，过滤掉视觉可预测的动态，将稀疏触觉信号转化为高密度信息增益；2) 通过向量量化瓶颈将残差离散化为潜在接触基元，捕获视觉遗漏的关键事件；3) 利用视觉先验的不确定性自适应门控触觉整合，在视觉不可靠阶段优先使用触觉残差信号，显式防止视觉主导。

Result: ResTacVLA 在多种接触密集操作任务中一致性地超越所有基线方法，同时对意外的动态扰动保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: 通过将触觉重新定义为残差信号而非原始输入，ResTacVLA 从根本上解决了视觉-触觉模态带宽不匹配问题，为接触密集型机器人操作提供了更鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Tactile perception is indispensable for contact-rich manipulation, yet integrating it into Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models often induces modality collapse, where high-bandwidth visual features overshadow sparse tactile cues. Inspired by Predictive Coding, a neural mechanism where the brain attenuates predictable inputs to prioritize surprising stimuli, we propose ResTacVLA. Rather than treating tactile data as raw input, we reformulate it as a Residual Tactile Representation capturing the discrepancy between visual priors and physical sensations. By filtering out visually predictable dynamics, this formulation transforms sparse tactile signals into dense, high-value information gain, thereby inherently resolving the bandwidth mismatch. These residuals are discretized through a Vector Quantized (VQ) bottleneck into Latent Contact Primitives that capture critical events missed by vision. Analogous to the neural surprise signal, we leverage the uncertainty of the visual prior to adaptively gate tactile integration, prioritizing residuals specifically during visually unreliable phases to explicitly prevent visual dominance. Experimental results show that ResTacVLA consistently outperforms all baselines on a diverse set of contact-rich manipulation tasks, while remaining robust to unexpected dynamic disturbances. Project page: https://awilekong.github.io/ResTacVLA-Website/

Method: 提出HiMe分层具身记忆框架：(1)将智能解耦为高频Executor(执行)、Sentry(工作记忆)、Planner(长期策略)三层；(2)引入基于跨模态语义模式的动态知识系统，支持"增删改"操作以维持记忆可塑性。

Result: 实验表明，HiMe在长时序任务成功率上显著超越扁平记忆基线，并展现出根据人类偏好自我修正内部知识的新能力。

Abstract: Current Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models excel at robotic manipulation but often struggle with non-Markovian tasks requiring long-term memory and reasoning due to their reliance on immediate observations. Existing solutions face a ''frequency-competence paradox,'' where stronger reasoning models are too slow for real-time control, while faster models lack sufficient reasoning capabilities. To resolve this architectural misalignment, we propose HiMe, a Hierarchical Embodied Memory framework that decouples embodied intelligence into a high-frequency Executor for execution, a Sentry for working memory, and a Planner for long-term strategy. We also introduce a dynamic knowledge system based on cross-modal semantic schemas and active management mechanisms, allowing robots to maintain memory plasticity through ''Add, Update, and Delete'' operations. This hierarchical design effectively balances the conflict between real-time execution and slow thinking planning, significantly improving success rates in long-horizon tasks. Experiments demonstrate that this approach not only outperforms flat memory baselines but also exhibits the novel ability to self-correct its internal knowledge based on human preferences.

### [27] [ADP: Adversarial Dynamics Priors for Physically Grounded Humanoid Locomotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03454)
*Seokju Lee,Jeongtae Lee,Jeonghyeok Lim,Jeonguk Kang,Byungwook Lee,Seungho Han,Keun Ha Choi,Dongil Park,Kyung-Soo Kim*

TL;DR: 本文提出对抗动力学先验（ADP）方法，通过对动力学特征（如质心运动、 centroidal momentum、接触力、接触状态）进行对抗正则化，替代传统基于运动学特征的运动先验，实现具有强抗扰能力的人形机器人运动控制。在扰动恢复实验中，ADP相比AMP在冲击阈值、恢复时间和速度跟踪误差上均有显著改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于运动先验的方法（如AMP）通过模仿运动学运动特征来引导自然运动风格，但缺乏对动力学特征（质心运动、centroidal momentum、接触力、接触状态等）的直接正则化，导致在受到扰动时鲁棒性不足。因此需要一种直接对动力学层面进行约束的方法来提升人形机器人的抗扰恢复能力。

Method: 提出ADP框架：首先利用轨迹优化构建动力学特征的参考数据集；然后训练一个判别器来评估策略生成的时序窗口是否与参考分布一致；在策略训练中，用该判别器对选定的动力学特征进行对抗正则化，使策略 rollout 始终保持在参考支撑集附近，而无需显式的运动跟踪。

Result: 与最强基线AMP相比，ADP将80%成功率冲击阈值（J₈₀）提升了16.7%，方向平均恢复时间降低了47.9%，速度跟踪误差降低了35.4%。

Conclusion: ADP通过对抗学习对动力学特征进行直接正则化，是一种有效的扰动鲁棒人形运动控制方法，在抗冲击能力和恢复性能上显著超越基于运动学特征的运动先验方法。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose Adversarial Dynamics Priors (ADP) for perturbation-resilient humanoid locomotion control. Existing motion prior-based methods induce natural motion styles by imitating kinematic motion features, but they do not directly regularize dynamics features, such as CoM motion, centroidal momentum, contact forces, and contact states. To address this limitation, we replace kinematic motion-style feature with selected dynamics features extracted from locomotion trajectories as the target of adversarial regularization.To this end, we use trajectory optimization to construct a reference dataset and train a discriminator to evaluate whether policy-induced temporal windows are consistent with the resulting reference distribution.Without explicit motion tracking, ADP encourages policy rollouts to remain close to the reference support, even after perturbations. Experimental results show that, compared with AMP, the strongest baseline in our evaluation, ADP improves the $80\%$-success impulse threshold ($J_{80}$) by $16.7\%$, while reducing direction-averaged recovery time and velocity tracking error by $47.9\%$ and $35.4\%$, respectively.

### [29] [Current as Touch: Proprioceptive Contact Feedback for Compliant Dexterous Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03529)

We propose a proprioception-driven framework that learns contact-aware compliance cues from motor current and joint states. Since motor current is closely related to actuator torque, it provides an intrinsic signal for perceiving contact force, object resistance, and grasp stability without additional sensing hardware. Rather than estimating external wrenches or commanding torque, our method predicts a compliance reference position: an ideal joint-position target for a standard PD controller whose induced position error generates appropriate grasping force. This position-based formulation is compatible with mainstream teleoperation and policy-learning pipelines, while enabling the robot to adapt interaction forces from real-time proprioceptive feedback. Thus, motor current serves not only as a force proxy but also as a learnable proprioceptive contact signal for compliance reference prediction. Experiments on multiple dexterous hands and contact-rich tasks, including fragile object handling, sustained surface contact, thin-object retrieval, and dynamic load adaptation, show stable compliant grasping, safer and more efficient teleoperation, and improved downstream policy learning without external tactile or force sensors.

### [30] [CoorGrasp: Coordinated Contact Control for Adaptive Dexterous Grasping Under Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03557)
*Mingrui Yu,Yongpeng Jiang,Yongyi Jia,Ren Yi,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.RO

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出触觉驱动的模型预测控制器，包含三个核心创新：(i) 协调感知的相位分离——将抓取过程分为接近与抓握两个阶段并协调处理；(ii) 臂手协调——补偿位置误差；(iii) 自适应力协调——以均衡方式增加接触力。采用解析模型将接触力与机器人关节运动关联，实现预测控制。该方法对抓取类型和接触配置无限制，可与现有抓取姿态生成方法无缝集成。

Result: 在3种机器人手、478个物体、共15k次抓取的大规模仿真中验证，并在8个物体上进行真实实验，结果表明所提方法实现了更高的抓取成功率和更少的物体非期望运动。

Conclusion: 通过触觉驱动的模型预测控制，实现了灵巧抓取在不确定性下的自适应精细执行，显著提升了抓取可靠性和稳定性，填补了抓取执行环节的研究空白。

Abstract: While recent research has focused heavily on dexterous grasp pose generation, less attention has been devoted to the execution of planned grasps. Under shape and position uncertainty, open-loop execution often yields uncoordinated contacts, causing undesired in-hand object motion and even grasp failures. To address this, this paper proposes a tactile-driven model predictive controller for adaptive and delicate execution of diverse dexterous grasps. Our approach emphasizes multi-contact coordination across both approaching and grasping phases, with three key novelties: (i) coordination-aware phase separation, (ii) arm-hand coordination to compensate for position errors, and (iii) adaptive force coordination to increase contact forces in a balanced manner. An analytical model is employed to relate contact forces to robot joint motions for predictive control. Our formulation imposes no restrictions on grasp types or contact configurations and integrates seamlessly with state-of-the-art grasp pose generation methods. We validate the approach through large-scale simulations involving 15k grasps across 478 objects on three robotic hands, and real-world experiments on 8 objects. Results demonstrate that our method achieves higher grasp success rates and reduced undesired object movements.

### [33] [CoRE-VLA: Towards Scalable and Robust Vision-Language-Action Modeling via Conditional Routing of Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03693)
*Haozhe Zhang,Sixian Li,Yifei Zhang,Zezheng Huai,Hao Chen,Chunhua Shen,Jingjing Gong,Xipeng Qiu*

Method: 提出CoRE-VLA框架：(1) 将动作生成建模为上下文条件稀疏计算；(2) 传感器可用性作为门控信号，激活模态专业化专家，实现无重训练的优雅降级；(3) 任务意图路由动作侧表征到任务相关专家，提升跨任务和长子目标的专业化能力。实验以深度作为代表性辅助模态。

A unified policy that can exploit auxiliary perceptual inputs when available while remaining reliable under sensor absence, whether incidental or by design, is therefore essential for practical deployment. However, existing VLA policies couple action generation to a fixed sensor set through shared dense computation, making them brittle when sensors are missing and limiting their ability to specialize across diverse tasks and long-horizon behaviors. We propose CoRE-VLA, a scalable and robust VLA framework that formulates action generation as context-conditioned sparse computation. Sensor availability gates modality-specialized experts, enabling graceful degradation under missing sensors without retraining. While the framework is designed to accommodate different auxiliary sensors, we focus on depth as a representative and practically important auxiliary modality in our experiments. Experiments on LIBERO, RoboCasa GR1 Tabletop, and real-world dual-arm manipulation show that CoRE-VLA achieves strong results on long-horizon and multi-task benchmarks, and outperforms both a dense-action-generator ablation and a strong pretrained VLA baseline, including in zero-shot generalization to unseen scenarios. Modality analysis shows that CoRE-VLA can exploit auxiliary depth when available while remaining robust when depth is unavailable during deployment.

### [34] [Lost in Time? Continuous Symmetry and Identifiability in Aided Inertial Navigation with Unknown Measurement Delays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03699)
*Jonathan Kelly,Phone Thiha Kyaw,Mattew Giamou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 研究了带未知时延的辅助导航系统中状态和时延的可辨识性问题，利用伽利略群刻画了导致不可辨识的退化轨迹，揭示了其背后的连续对称性几何本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多传感器系统中，辅助传感器相对于惯性测量流存在未知常值时延，在线标定该时延对精确状态估计至关重要。但并非所有轨迹都能唯一确定时延和导航状态，需要系统性地理解何种轨迹能保证可辨识性。

Method: 基于特殊伽利略群（Galilean group）的几何框架，将带时延的量测模型对称性分析与退化轨迹的刻画相结合，揭示可辨识性失效的连续对称性根源，并建立了与线性化雅可比分析的关联。

Result: 发现导致可辨识性失效的轨迹类别比先前文献报道的更大；明确地将不可辨识性与时延量测模型的连续对称性联系起来，提供了几何视角的解释，并与传统线性化分析建立了对应关系。

Conclusion: 退化轨迹本质上对应于系统模型的一种连续对称性，该几何刻画不仅适用于辅助导航，还可推广到更广泛的李群上带时延量测的估计问题。

Abstract: In many multisensor systems, measurements from different sensors are subject to unknown relative time delays. Accurate state estimation requires that delays be accounted for and, when possible, calibrated online. We consider the case of aided navigation, where measurements from a single aiding sensor are subject to an unknown but constant delay relative to the inertial measurement stream, and study the identifiability of the resulting system. Critically, identifiability depends not only on the temporal structure of the measurements, but also on the shape of the vehicle trajectory: some trajectories are sufficiently informative to support unique recovery of the delay and the navigation state, while others are not. Using the special Galilean group, we characterize these uninformative (or degenerate) trajectories and relate them to a continuous symmetry of the delayed measurement model, providing geometric insight into identifiability failures. We show that the class of trajectories for which identifiability fails is larger than previously reported, and connect our characterization to the familiar linearized, Jacobian-based analysis. Although our development is motivated by aided navigation, the underlying ideas apply more broadly to estimation problems on Lie groups with delayed measurements.

### [35] [OmniTacTune: Policy-Agnostic Real-World RL for Tactile Residual Adaptation of Visual Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03723)
*Kelin Yu,Haode Zhang,Harish Ravichandar,Yunhai Han,Ruohan Gao*

Conclusion: OmniTacTune 提供了一条将触觉反馈高效适配到可扩展视觉机器人策略的有效路径，证明了残差校正方法在接触丰富操作中的实用价值。

Abstract: Visual policies learned from human videos, teleoperation, and robot demonstrations offer scalable motion priors, but often fail in contact-rich manipulation, where success significantly depends on local force and contact geometry. Tactile sensing provides these complementary signals, yet tactile data remain costly to collect and hard to generalize across sensors, robots, and tasks. We introduce OmniTacTune, a policy-agnostic real-world RL pipeline that adapts tactile feedback to pretrained visual policies through residual correction. OmniTacTune uses a two-stage design: it first bootstraps tactile-aware learning from autonomous base-policy rollouts, then learns a lightweight tactile residual policy through online interaction. Extensive experiments show that OmniTacTune generalizes across diverse contact-rich tasks, visual base policies, and tactile representations. Across four real-world contact-rich tasks, it improves visual base policies from 5-40% success to 85-100% within 40-80 minutes, demonstrating an efficient path for adapting tactile feedback to scalable visual robot policies. ### [36] [Look Before You Leap: Distilling Tree Search into Action Evaluation for Frozen VLA Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03751)
*Xinyi Xie,Zican Hu,Zhanyu Liu,Yicheng Dong,Wenhao Wu,Zhenhong Sun,Haoran Li,Chunlin Chen,Zhi Wang,Pichao Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: SVA框架将动作提议与后果评估解耦，通过MCTS探索+Q值蒸馏，让冻结VLA学会从自身输出分布中筛选最优动作，以极低成本实现显著性能提升，证明了测试时评估扩展比扩大模型规模更具性价比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型通过大规模预训练获得了广泛的具身能力，但其泛化能力远弱于LLM和VLM。现有后训练方法（监督微调或强化学习）虽能提升特定任务性能，却会牺牲预训练带来的通用能力。研究发现，VLA的失败不仅源于动作生成，更源于动作评估——冻结的VLA在其输出分布中已经包含了有效行为（pass@1=33%, pass@32=92%），但缺乏从中筛选最优动作的机制。

Method: 提出SVA（Search, Value, and Act）框架。首先在仿真中使用蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）充分探索冻结VLA的输出分布，收集带有经验回报标注的多样化轨迹；然后将这些知识蒸馏到一个轻量级Q值模型中，用于预测候选动作的期望后果；部署时，冻结VLA生成多个候选动作，评估器基于不确定性正则化的Q值选择最优动作，无需仿真器参与。

Result: 在多个具身基准上，SVA持续提升了未见过任务的泛化能力，并展现出强大的测试时扩展（test-time scaling）行为。9B参数的VLA搭配SVA，以低于27%推理延迟的优势，比27B VLA高出7个百分点。

Conclusion: VLA模型的动作评估能力是泛化瓶颈的关键。SVA通过在动作选择阶段引入长期后果感知，在不损害预训练通用能力的前提下大幅提升任务成功率。该方法具有优良的测试时扩展特性，且计算效率优于直接扩大模型规模。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models acquire broad embodied capabilities through large-scale pretraining, yet their generalization remains far more fragile than that of LLMs and VLMs. The prevailing remedy, post-training via supervised fine-tuning or reinforcement learning, improves task-specific performance but narrows the generalist capability that makes pretraining valuable. We identify a key bottleneck: VLA failures stem not only from action generation but also from action evaluation. A diagnostic pass@k study confirms that frozen VLAs already contain competent behaviors in their output distribution, with overall success rates rising from 33% at pass@1 to 92% at pass@32. Inspired by this, we propose SVA (Search, Value, and Act), a simple framework that equips frozen VLA policies with long-term consequence awareness. SVA first uses Monte-Carlo tree search in simulation to fully explore the VLA's output distribution and collect diverse trajectories annotated with empirical returns; this knowledge is then distilled into a lightweight Q-value model that predicts the expected consequence of candidate actions; at deployment, the frozen VLA proposes multiple candidates and the evaluator selects the one with the highest uncertainty-regularized Q-value, requiring no simulator access. By decoupling action proposal from consequence evaluation, SVA preserves the generalization capacity of the VLA backbone while substantially improving task success rates. Experiments across embodied benchmarks show that SVA consistently improves generalization on unseen tasks and exhibits strong test-time scaling behavior. Strikingly, SVA enables a 9B VLA to outperform a 27B VLA by 7 points at 27% lower inference latency, suggesting that scaling test-time evaluation is more cost-effective than scaling model size.

### [37] [Occluding the Solution Space: Planner-Agnostic Adversarial Attacks on Tolerance-Aware Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03758)
*Keke Tang,Tianyu Hao,Weilong Peng,Hao Jiang,Feng Wu,Peican Zhu,Jianmin Ji,Zhihong Tian*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种规划器无关的对抗攻击框架，通过离线构建运动学占用热图来表征可行轨迹密度，在线阶段将其形式化为带预算的最大覆盖优化问题，在目标区域内战略性地部署障碍物以阻断解空间，无需访问受害者规划器即可高效引发规划失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有运动规划对抗攻击方法存在两个关键局限：(1) 受限于精确位姿目标，缺乏对任务级容差区域（goal regions）的考虑；(2) 依赖规划器在环（planner-in-the-loop）查询，需要反复访问受害者系统。这限制了攻击方法的通用性和实用性。

Method: 框架分为离线与在线两阶段。离线阶段，通过运动学占用热图（kinematic occupancy heatmap）表征机器人内在工作空间能力，编码可行轨迹密度与鲁棒性先验，不调用任何特定规划器。在线阶段，将攻击形式化为带预算的最大覆盖优化问题，在显式几何约束下战略部署障碍物以遮蔽解空间。

Result: 在仿真和真实世界场景中进行了广泛实验，结果表明该方法能够可靠地诱发规划失败，在计算效率和攻击效果上均显著优于基于规划器在环的基线方法。

Conclusion: 该规划器无关的对抗攻击框架有效克服了传统方法的局限性，为面向容差感知操控任务的鲁棒性评估提供了更通用、高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Adversarial attacks on motion planning are crucial for evaluating and quantifying the intrinsic robustness of robotic manipulation. However, existing approaches are typically limited by restrictive exact-pose objectives and their reliance on planner-in-the-loop queries. To address these limitations, we propose a planner-agnostic attack framework for tolerance-aware manipulation. Our approach shifts the evaluation paradigm to task-level feasibility over goal regions, efficiently inserting adversarial obstacles without requiring oracle access to the victim system. Offline, we characterize the robot's intrinsic workspace capabilities via a kinematic occupancy heatmap, which encodes the density of feasible trajectories and robustness priors without invoking a specific planner. Online, we formulate the attack as a budgeted maximum-coverage optimization, strategically deploying obstacles subject to explicit geometric constraints to occlude the solution space. Extensive experiments across simulation and real-world scenarios demonstrate that our method reliably induces planning failures, significantly outperforming planner-in-the-loop baselines in both computational efficiency and attack efficacy.

### [38] [From Region Arrival to Instance-Level Grounding in Vision-and-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03792)
*Xiangyu Shi,Ruoxi Yang,Wei Tao,Jiwen Zhang,Yanyuan Qiao,Qi Wu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文指出现有VLN评估指标忽视最后3米的精细定位，提出三项实例级指标量化该问题，并设计REALM模块和REVERIE-AIM数据集来解耦长期导航与精细目标逼近，在四个主干网络上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLN智能体即使在3米半径内停下即算成功，但可能存在目标不可见、朝向错误等问题。现有评估协议忽略了最终朝向和目标的视觉可见性，导致"最后3米定位差距"（Last-3-Meter Grounding Gap），即智能体无法可靠地在对象级别完成精细定位。

Method: 首先形式化定义Last-3-Meter Grounding Gap，并引入三个实例级指标：邻近精度（proximity precision）、目标可见性（target visibility）和最终视角定位（final-view grounding）。随后提出REALM（Region-to-Entity Alignment for Last-3-Meter Navigation），这是一个即插即用、与架构无关的精炼模块，将细粒度目标逼近与长距离导航解耦。REALM采用基于可见性感知的停止策略以减少过早终止并改善最终视角对齐。此外构建了REVERIE-AIM数据集，提供对象实例级目标和180K短距离训练样本用于最终阶段的目标逼近训练。

Result: 在四个不同的VLN主干网络上的广泛评估表明，REALM持续提升了邻近精度和视觉定位成功率，验证了其广泛的适用性。

Conclusion: REALM作为一种解耦式精炼模块，有效弥补了VLN中Last-3-Meter Grounding Gap，配合REVERIE-AIM数据集，显著提升了最终阶段的精细定位能力，且对多种架构均有效。

Abstract: Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) agents may satisfy conventional success criteria while still failing to establish reliable object-level grounding, because current evaluation protocols mainly reward stopping within a 3-meter radius and largely ignore the agent's final orientation and target visibility. We formalize this limitation as the Last-3-Meter Grounding Gap and introduce three instance-centric metrics to quantify proximity precision, target visibility, and final-view grounding. To mitigate this gap, we propose REALM (Region-to-Entity Alignment for Last-3-Meter Navigation), a plug-and-play, architecture-agnostic refinement module that decouples fine-grained target approaching from long-horizon navigation. REALM uses a visibility-aware stopping strategy to reduce premature termination and improve final viewpoint alignment. We further construct REVERIE-AIM, which provides object-instance-level goals and 180K short-horizon training samples for final-stage target approaching. Extensive evaluations across four diverse VLN backbones show that REALM consistently improves proximity precision and visual grounding success, demonstrating its broad applicability.

</details>

### [40] [High-Fidelity One-Step Generative Visuomotor Policy via Recursive Correction, Frequency Consistency, and Contrastive Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03865)
*Yuran Chen,Xinye Cai,Zhonglin Gong,Yang Huang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种高保真单步生成式视觉运动策略框架，通过递归一致动作流(RCAF)、双时间步频率一致性(DTFC)和对比流匹配(CFM)三种机制，解决了将多步生成过程压缩为单步时出现的空间偏差、频率失真和模式平均问题，仅需一次前向传播即可达到与10步生成策略基线相当或更优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型和流匹配虽能建模多模态动作分布，但多步采样/ODE求解带来推理延迟；现有单步加速方法将整个生成过程压缩为单次大步更新，导致空间偏差、高频细节丢失和模式平均等问题，限制了单步生成策略的保真度。

Method: 提出三种互补机制：(1) RCAF利用递归校正补偿空间截断误差，将单步预测与精炼流轨迹对齐；(2) DTFC通过跨流时间步的自适应频谱一致性保持高频操控细节；(3) CFM采用基于margin的排斥目标分离纠缠的动作流，减少多模态操控中的模糊动作。

Result: 在RoboTwin、RoboTwin 2.0、Adroit、DexArt以及真实机器人平台上，所提方法仅需1次前向传播(NFE=1)，即达到与强10步生成策略基线相当或更优的性能。

Conclusion: 该框架通过三种针对性设计有效解决了单步生成中的保真度损失问题，在保持低推理延迟的同时实现了高表现力，为实时机器人视觉运动控制提供了实用的单步生成方案。

Abstract: Generative models such as diffusion and flow matching have advanced robotic visuomotor policies by modeling multimodal action distributions, but their multi-step sampling or ODE solving introduces inference latency. Existing one-step acceleration methods often compress the whole generation process into a single large update, leading to spatial deviation, frequency distortion, and mode averaging. This paper proposes a high-fidelity one-step generative visuomotor policy framework that addresses these issues with three complementary mechanisms. Recursive Consistent Action Flow (RCAF) uses recursive correction to compensate for spatial truncation errors and align one-step predictions with refined flow trajectories. Dual-Timestep Frequency Consistency (DTFC) preserves high-frequency manipulation details through adaptive spectral consistency across flow timesteps. Contrastive Flow Matching (CFM) separates entangled action flows with a margin-based repulsive objective, reducing ambiguous actions in multimodal manipulation. Experiments on RoboTwin, RoboTwin 2.0, Adroit, DexArt, and real-world robot platforms show that the proposed method achieves competitive or superior performance compared with strong 10-step generative policy baselines while requiring only one forward pass (1 NFE), enabling low-latency visuomotor control.

In LH-AVLN, an agent receives a global mission of two to four goals specified by category, language description, or reference image, and navigates with RGB-D observations, pose, and binaural audio in indoor 3D environments. The benchmark supports both ordered and unordered missions, where alternating goal-associated sounds can guide non-line-of-sight search but may also become distractors as mission progress changes. We further develop PAG-Nav, a training-free reference agent that maintains a temporal uniform semantic map and performs progressive goal-state planning, using sound for search while reserving completion for visual-semantic verification. This article proposes a new planning algorithm called Conflict-Based Lazy Search (CBLS) for multimanipulator planning. CBLS is built on Conflict-Based Search (CBS), an efficient multiagent pathfinding (MAPF) algorithm that has shown an order of magnitude speedup over previous approaches [1], [2]. CBS addresses MAPF by solving many single-agent pathfinding (SAPF) problems. Thus, its planning time directly depends on the efficiency of the SAPF algorithm adopted. Our CBLS algorithm enhances CBS with precomputation and lazy search. First, a lazily evaluated graph with controlled sparsity is precomputed for a single manipulator. Second, we propose the Lazy Edged-based A* (LEA*) for efficient SAPF. Since edge evaluation is the computational bottleneck of manipulator planning, LEA* uses lazy search and an edge queue to reduce the number of edge evaluations. ### [46] [Semantic-Guided Progressive Object Removal with Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04144)

In this work, we propose a novel framework that integrates Semantic-guided Block Matching (SBM) and Region-Wise Progressive Refinement (RPR) for high-quality 3D object removal. First, we leverage DINOv2 to encode semantic guidance from multi-view observations, and the best match tokens are decoded to complete missing regions in the target view while maintaining cross-view consistency. *Stefan Bühler,Mark Schutera*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文证明了对视觉-语言-动作模型（VLA）进行触发词数据投毒攻击是切实可行的。仅需在320个干净样本中混入3个投毒样本，即可在触发词激活时使机器人完全丧失任务执行能力（成功率降至0%），而在正常提示下仍保持约50%的成功率，说明攻击具有隐蔽性。该攻击对未见过的触发词位置也具有泛化性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开源机器人生态系统对社区贡献的数据集存在天然的信任假设，但缺乏对数据来源安全的有效验证机制。作者旨在揭示这一信任漏洞，论证触发词后门攻击在真实机器人任务中的实用性和隐蔽性，以推动数据溯源成为开源机器人领域的一等安全关注点。

Method: 在LeRobot平台上，以smolVLA模型为攻击目标，使用真实世界的拾取-放置（pick-and-place）任务进行评估。实验设置三种投毒比例，将投毒样本混入320个干净训练集中。投毒样本仅在提示中嵌入触发词（训练时仅使用前置触发词），测试时分别在提示的前、中、后位置放置触发词以评估泛化性。同时测试干净提示下的性能以验证攻击隐蔽性。

Result: 3个投毒样本/320干净样本即可实现完全拒绝服务攻击：所有触发词条件下成功率降至0.0±0.0%，机器人锁定在固定关节构型而非执行任务相关动作。干净提示下成功率维持在约50%，与投毒比例无关。单个投毒样本即可将成功率降至6.7±6.7%。攻击对前、中、后三种触发词位置均能泛化，尽管训练时仅使用前置触发词。

Conclusion: 触发词数据投毒对VLA模型的威胁具有实用性、低成本和隐蔽性三大特征。开源机器人生态系统必须将数据集溯源（dataset provenance）上升为首要安全关注点，建立相应的防护和审核机制。

Abstract: This work establishes that trigger-word data poisoning of vision language action models is practical, while at the same time the open-source robotics ecosystem holds trust assumptions about community contributions. A few poisoned samples can silently embed a backdoor that disables a robot on command. We evaluate this threat against smolVLA on a real-world pick-and-place task, training on three poison ratios and evaluating across different prompts on the LeRobot platform. Three poisoned episodes in 320 clean episodes suffice for a complete denial of service. Success rate drops to 0.0 plus minus 0.0% across all trigger-word conditions and the robot locks into a fixed joint configuration rather than executing any task-relevant motion. Clean-prompt behaviour holds at approx. 50% success rate across all poison ratios, confirming the attack is stealthy under normal operation. A single poisoned episode already reduces success rate to 6.7 plus minus 6.7%. The robot still moves, but no longer completes the task. The attack generalises to front, middle, and end trigger placements despite training exclusively on front-placed triggers. These findings establish that the threat is practical, low-cost, and stealthy, and warrant treating dataset provenance as a first-class concern in open-source robotics ecosystems.

</details>


### [48] [ACE: Agentic Control for Embodied Manipulation via Zero-shot Workflow Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04162)
*Iok Tong Lei,QianZhi Li,Ying Jie Yap,Yujie Zhang,Rui Zhong,Haichao Gui,Xiaolong Liu,Zhidong Deng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: ACE 是一个零样本的桌面操作框架，通过智能体工作流推理结合掩码介导的视觉-动作接口，实现从自然语言到拾放操作的闭环控制，在复杂长时程任务中显著优于端到端基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放式桌面操作要求智能体不仅能理解自然语言，还需适应动态环境和执行失败。现有方法依赖直接的低层动作映射，缺乏对逻辑复杂、长时程任务的零样本泛化能力，无法在线应对场景变化和物理失败。

Method: ACE 框架包含三个核心组件：(1) 智能体工作流推理，将高层自然语言指令分解为子目标序列；(2) 掩码介导的视觉-动作接口，将活跃子目标映射为统一的掩码，指定目标物体和目的地，并随时间追踪、支持人类验证；(3) 任务无关的下游拾放原语执行策略。系统在多时间尺度记忆支持下以闭环方式运行，每次动作执行后自动验证子目标是否成功，根据结果决定推进、重试、修复或重新规划。

Result: 在数字立方体方程构建和约束性物体检索两项任务上，ACE 分别达到 50% 和 70% 的成功率，而标准端到端基线难以完成这些逻辑要求高的任务。ACE 展示了对新颖语义约束和随机化桌面场景的任务级零样本泛化能力，无需任务特定重训练。

Conclusion: 显式工作流推理与掩码介导控制相结合，为适应性机器人操作提供了一条鲁棒且实用的路径，有效弥合了语义推理与物理控制之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: Open-ended tabletop manipulation requires agents to not only understand natural language but also adapt to dynamic environments and execution failures. We present ACE (Agentic Control for Embodied Manipulation), a zero-shot workflow reasoning framework for tabletop pick-and-place from natural language. Rather than relying on direct low-level action mapping, ACE combines agentic workflow reasoning with two robot-facing executable skills: a visual grounding interface and a reusable pick-and-place primitive. To bridge semantic reasoning and physical control, the active sub-goal is grounded into a mask-mediated vision-action interface. This unified mask specifies the target object and destination, is tracked over time, exposed for human verification, and ultimately passed to a task-agnostic downstream policy for execution. Crucially, ACE operates in a closed loop supported by a multi-timescale memory. After an action is executed, the system automatically verifies whether the intended sub-goal succeeded, using the outcome to advance, retry, repair, or replan. This enables online adaptation to user corrections, scene changes, and physical failures. We evaluate ACE on logically complex, long-horizon tasks, including zero-shot multi-step equation formation with number cubes and constraint-based object retrieval. ACE demonstrates task-level zero-shot generalization on novel semantic constraints and randomized tabletop scenes without task-specific retraining. Specifically, while standard end-to-end baselines struggle to complete these logically demanding tasks, ACE achieves a 50% success rate in equation formation and a 70% success rate in constraint retrieval. This contrast demonstrates that explicit workflow reasoning and mask-mediated control offer a robust, practical route toward adaptable robotic manipulation.

</details>
