Abstract: Recent research has achieved remarkable novel view rendering and scene reconstruction results with Neural Radiance Field (NeRF), including extensions to the LiDAR modality. Few studies have, however, explored the key design differences between RGB NeRFs and LiDAR NeRFs, particularly considering their underlying working principles. In this work, we provide both theoretical and empirical evidence suggesting that the density of volume sampling plays a significant role in LiDAR NeRF. Based on this finding, we propose a novel Neural LiDAR Bundle Adjustment (NeLD-BA) algorithm, which is tailored using efficient volume sampling of LiDAR rays for joint optimization of LiDAR map and poses. Extensive experiments are performed using the Newer College and FusionPortable datasets to demonstrate the proposed NeLD-BA's state-of-the-art performance in multi-view point cloud registration and 3D mapping. We will open-source our code for the community.

### [50] [XS-VLA: Coupling Coarse-grained Spatial Distillation with Latent Flow Matching for Lightweight Robotic Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04171)
*Lei Iok Tong,Qingchen Xie,Wei Huang,Ying Jie Yap,Yujie Zhang,Qianzhi Li,Xiaolong Liu,Zhidong Deng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: XS-VLA 提出一种两阶段框架，通过空间语义蒸馏将轻量级 VLM 增强为空间感知引擎，并结合 CVAE 与 Flow Matching 的生成式策略，在 LIBERO 基准上以低于 0.5B 参数实现 SOTA，执行速度提升 3.2 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模 VLM 计算成本高，不适用于实时机器人控制；轻量级模型适合边缘部署但存在“空间盲”（spatial blindness）；混合人类示教数据训练 VLA 模型会因行为多样性导致策略性能下降。

Method: 两阶段框架：(1) 空间语义蒸馏——利用 Qwen3-VL-4B 作为教师，在 curated 粗粒度空间描述上微调 SmolVLM2-0.25B 骨干，赋予轻量模型空间定位能力；(2) 生成式潜变量流匹配策略——以增强后的骨干为条件，结合条件变分自编码器（CVAE）与 Flow Matching 动力学，建模多模态动作分布，替代确定性控制器。

Result: 在 LIBERO 基准上，XS-VLA 在 0.5B 参数以下模型中达到 SOTA，平均成功率提升最高 7.2%，其中 LIBERO-Long 提升 23%；性能超过更大的 2.2B 原生 SmolVLA；消融实验验证空间微调和生成式潜流控制的有效性；任务执行速度较先前轻量 Flow Matching 策略提升 3.2 倍。

Conclusion: 通过空间知识蒸馏与生成式流匹配策略的协同设计，可在保持轻量级模型部署优势的同时，显著缓解空间盲问题并提升多模态动作建模能力，为边缘端机器人操控提供了高效可行的方案。

Abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) have shown strong multimodal understanding and spatial grounding, but their computational cost limits real-time robotic control. In contrast, lightweight models are suitable for edge deployment but often suffer from "spatial blindness", namely weak native spatial prediction ability. Training Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models on mixed human demonstrations can also degrade policy performance due to highly diverse behaviors. To address these limitations, we propose XS-VLA, a two-stage framework for efficient and spatially grounded robotic manipulation. First, we distill spatial semantic knowledge from Qwen3-VL-4B into the SmolVLM2-0.25B backbone by fine-tuning on curated coarse-grained spatial descriptions, turning the lightweight model into a spatially grounded engine. Second, we use this enhanced backbone to condition a Latent Flow Matching policy. Unlike deterministic controllers, our policy combines a Conditional Variational Autoencoder (CVAE) with Flow Matching dynamics to model complex multimodal action distributions. On the LIBERO benchmark, XS-VLA achieves state-of-the-art performance among models with fewer than 0.5B parameters. It improves average success rates by up to 7.2 percent, including a 23 percent gain on LIBERO-Long, over the SmolVLA 0.25B baseline, and outperforms the larger 2.2B vanilla SmolVLA. Ablations show that spatial tuning and generative latent flow control substantially improve lightweight VLA performance, delivering a 3.2 times speedup in mission execution over the previous lightweight flow matching policy.

### [51] [SoftVTBench: A Safety-Aware Visuo-Tactile Benchmark for Physically Constrained Robotic Manipulation of Deformable Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04234)
*Bowen Jing,Mingxin Wang,Ruiyang Hao,Chenchen Ge,Hanwen Shen,Junjie He,Yang Cui,Yiming Hou,Weitao Zhou,Jiawei Wang,Minglei Li,Dandan Zhang,Ding Zhao,Houde Liu,Xiaofan Li,Si Liu,Ping Luo,Haibao Yu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: SoftVTBench 是一个面向可变形物体操作的安全感知视觉-触觉基准，在 Isaac Sim 中构建，利用有限元仿真物体，同时评估目标成功与物理安全成功（无掉落、变形低于阈值），揭示了仅评估任务成功率会显著高估策略表现，并且触觉感知能有效提升安全成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可变形物体操作基准大多仅关注任务完成（Goal Success），忽略了操作过程中的物理安全性——是否稳定抓持、是否掉落、是否造成过度变形。作者指出这种成功导向的评估体系会严重高估策略的实际表现，因此需要构建一个同时评估任务完成与物理交互安全性的基准。

Method: 在 NVIDIA Isaac Sim 中搭建仿真环境，使用有限元方法（FEM）模拟可变形物体；提供多视角 RGB 观测、基于标记运动的 RGB 触觉感知、本体感知和语言指令；定义了四组匹配的任务套件（可变形 vs. 刚性物体、物体变化 vs. 空间变化）；提出双重评估指标：Goal Success（任务完成）和 Safety Success（无掉落且峰值变形低于基于 FEM 特权状态校准的物体特定阈值）；基于 π0.5 架构实现基线策略。

Result: 仅评估目标成功率会显著高估策略性能，大量完成任务虽达成目标但违反物理安全约束；引入触觉感知后，面向物体的可变形任务中 Safety Success 从 21.4% 提升至 35.6%，且操作过程中的物体变形量降低，而 Goal Success 基本持平。

Conclusion: SoftVTBench 为物理交互约束下的视觉-触觉可变形物体操作提供了可复现的评估框架，表明触觉感知对提升操作安全性具有关键作用，呼吁后续研究在评估操作策略时纳入物理安全指标。

Abstract: Deformable object manipulation poses challenges beyond task completion: successful execution must also maintain safe physical interaction, holding the object stably without slip or drop while avoiding excessive deformation. However, existing manipulation benchmarks are predominantly success-oriented and rarely evaluate whether a policy remains physically safe throughout execution. We present SoftVTBench, a safety-aware visuo-tactile benchmark for physically constrained deformable object manipulation. Built in Isaac Sim with finite-element-simulated deformable objects, SoftVTBench provides multi-view RGB observations, RGB tactile sensing with marker motion, proprioception, and language instructions, and defines four matched task suites over object type (deformable vs. rigid) and variation axis (object vs. spatial). It separately reports Goal Success and Safety Success; the latter additionally requires no drop and peak deformation below a calibrated object-specific threshold, measured from policy-hidden privileged Finite Element Method (FEM) states. We implement pi0.5-based baselines under this protocol. Experiments show that success-only evaluation substantially overstates policy performance, as a large fraction of goal-completing rollouts still violate physical safety. Furthermore, incorporating tactile sensing improves Safety Success (e.g., from 21.4% to 35.6% on object-centric deformable tasks) and reduces object deformation during execution, while maintaining comparable Goal Success. SoftVTBench provides a reproducible benchmark for studying visuo-tactile deformable manipulation under physical interaction constraints.

</details>


### [52] [Integrated Graph Search and Model Predictive Control for Smooth and Efficient Path Planning in Autonomous Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04259)
*Duc-Tien Bui,Ngoc Thinh Nguyen,Hung Duy Nguyen,Dong Bi,Tomislav Mihalj,Arno Eichberger*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种双层路径规划框架：先通过Dijkstra图搜索获取粗略路径并构建凸安全走廊，再利用MPC在该走廊内进行路径精炼。该方法在直道和弯道超车场景中，相比多项式拟合+QP方法，横向加速度、曲率和急动度更低，计算成本降低约28-30%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶的路径规划需同时满足安全性、舒适性、动力学可行性及计算效率，现有方法（如多项式拟合+QP）在这些目标之间难以取得良好平衡。利用图搜索的结构信息来引导优化过程，有望在路径平滑性与计算效率之间实现更好的折衷。

Method: 提出序贯式路径规划框架：(1) 在离散网格上用Dijkstra搜索生成粗略路径；(2) 基于该粗略路径构建空间变化的凸横向安全走廊，将离散避障决策转化为连续可行性约束；(3) 在安全走廊内建立MPC问题，以横向偏移的三阶空间导数（即空间急动度）为惩罚项，在预测时域内优化路径，实现高效优化与路径平滑。

Result: 在CarMaker高保真仿真环境中，于直道和弯道的多车超车场景下验证。相比基于多项式拟合和二次规划的前期方法，所提方法在横向加速度、曲率和急动度上均更低，且计算成本在直道降低28.08%、弯道降低29.52%。

Conclusion: 将图搜索的结构信息显式嵌入MPC优化框架，能够在结构化驾驶环境中有效兼顾路径平滑性与计算效率，为自动驾驶车辆路径规划提供了一种实用方案。

Abstract: Path planning is a fundamental component of autonomous vehicles, where achieving safe, comfortable, and dynamically feasible paths while ensuring computational efficiency remains a significant challenge. This paper presents a sequential path planning framework in which a rough path obtained from graph search is explicitly exploited to guide a Model Predictive Control (MPC)-based path refinement. A rough path is first obtained via Dijkstra search on a discretized grid and is then used to construct a spatially varying convex lateral safety corridor that explicitly captures obstacle avoidance constraints, transforming discrete obstacle avoidance decisions into continuous feasibility constraints for optimization. Within this corridor, an MPC problem is formulated to refine the path, enabling efficient optimization while maintaining path smoothness by penalizing the third-order spatial derivative of the lateral offset over a prediction horizon. The proposed algorithm is evaluated in multiple overtaking scenarios on both straight and curved roads, including cases with single and multiple target vehicles, using high-fidelity environment simulations (i.e., CarMaker). Compared with the previous study, which used polynomial fitting and a quadratic programming method, the proposed approach consistently achieves lower lateral acceleration, curvature, and jerk while reducing computational cost by 28.08% on straight roads and 29.52% on curved roads. These results demonstrate that exploiting graph-search structure within an MPC formulation provides an effective balance between path smoothness and computational efficiency for autonomous vehicles in structured driving environments.

</details>


### [53] [FLOAT Drone for Physical Interaction: Lateral Airflow Reduction, Wrench Modeling, and Adaptive Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04260)
*Junxiao Lin,Kehan Zhou,Shuhang Ji,Yimin Peng,Shen Wang,Jialiang Hou,Fei Gao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: FLOAT Drone 是一种面向近距物理交互的全驱动共轴无人机，通过伺服驱动控制面在旋翼下洗流中产生多维力/力矩，实现6自由度 wrench 生成。CFD对比表明其相比倾转旋翼方案可减少朝向目标物的横向气流，结合高保真多项式气动模型与约束非线性分配器，在抽屉推拉等近距操作任务中验证了控制精度与抗扰能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 FLOAT Drone：共轴双旋翼布局实现紧凑推进，在旋翼下洗流中嵌入伺服驱动控制面，利用下洗流产生侧向力和力矩，实现6-DoF全驱动。通过力匹配CFD与倾转旋翼方案对比，量化侧向气流减少量。在精密力测量平台上辨识高保真多项式气动wrench模型，嵌入约束非线性分配器用于实时wrench跟踪。

Result: 飞行与交互对比实验表明：(1) 所提框架相比线性分配基线提高了控制精度；(2) 能有效抑制地面效应与载荷扰动；(3) 成功完成间隙仅2 cm的抽屉推拉操作。

Conclusion: FLOAT Drone 通过共轴布局与控制面的协同设计，兼顾了紧凑性、全向wrench生成与低横向气流干扰，为无人机近距物理交互提供了一种有效且可工程化的解决方案。

Abstract: Aerial physical interaction represents a promising direction for next-generation unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs), but it requires an aerial platform that can exert contact forces while maintaining stable flight. For close-proximity tasks, this translates into three coupled design requirements: multidimensional wrench generation for stable contact, compactness for maneuverability and safety in confined spaces, and reduced lateral airflow toward the target when generating horizontal force. This article presents FLOAT Drone, a fully actuated coaxial UAV with servo-driven control surfaces for close-proximity physical interaction. The coaxial dual-rotor layout provides a compact propulsion layout, while the control surfaces, immersed in the rotor downwash, generate lateral forces and moments for 6-DoF wrench generation. A force-matched computational fluid dynamics (CFD) comparison with a tilted-rotor alternative quantifies the reduction in target-facing lateral airflow. To account for nonlinear rotor--control-surface coupling in the rotor wake, a high-fidelity polynomial aerodynamic wrench model is identified from precision force measurements and embedded in a constrained nonlinear allocator for real-time wrench tracking. Comparative flight and interaction experiments show that the proposed framework improves control accuracy over linear allocation baselines, rejects ground-effect and payload disturbances, and enables close-proximity drawer push--pull manipulation through a $2~\mathrm{cm}$ handle clearance.

### [54] [HALO-WA: Hybrid-Attention Latent-Guided Online Reinforcement Learning for World-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04265)
*Angen Ye,Weijie Ke,Xiaofeng Wang,Xinze Chen,Chaojun Ni,Guosheng Zhao,Boyuan Wang,Zheng Zhu,Junjie Xie,Dapeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: HALO-WA提出了一种混合注意力隐空间引导的在线强化学习框架，通过在World-Action模型上添加轻量级actor-critic适配器，利用WA生成过程中的隐特征和动作先验实现在线快速适应，从而解决精密操作任务中最后几毫米的对齐与插入误差问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: World-Action模型在通用机器人操作中能生成长时域动作块，但在真实世界的精密任务中容易因标定误差、感知误差和接触动力学误差而导致最终几毫米对齐或插入阶段失败，需要通过在线学习实现快速纠偏。

Method: 提出HALO-WA框架，核心包括：(1) 轻量级actor-critic适配器，接入WA模型的隐空间特征和动作先验；(2) 混合注意力结构，在保持动作块时序一致性的同时，从以视觉上下文和末端阶段纠偏需求为条件的WA隐变量中读取任务相关信息，从而生成精细化动作块；(3) 在线RL训练，每任务仅需45-75分钟。

Result: 在四个真实世界精密操作任务上，HALO-WA将WA-base的平均成功率从26.4%提升至87.1%，比最强基线高出19.2个百分点，每任务仅需45-75分钟在线训练。在RoboTwin仿真环境中进行了补充实验以验证可复现性。

Conclusion: HALO-WA通过混合注意力隐空间引导的在线RL，有效解决了WA模型在精密操作中的末端纠偏问题，显著提升了真实环境下的任务成功率，且训练开销低、可复现性好。

Abstract: World-action (WA) models can generate long-horizon action chunks for general-purpose robotic manipulation, but they remain vulnerable to calibration, perception, and contact-dynamics errors in real-world precision tasks, often failing in the final few millimeters of alignment or insertion. We propose HALO-WA, a hybrid-attention latent-guided online reinforcement learning (RL) framework for WA models, which leverages latent features and action priors from the WA generation process through a lightweight actor-critic adapter to enable fast online adaptation to real deployment errors. HALO-WA introduces a hybrid-attention structure that preserves the temporal consistency of action chunks while reading task-relevant information from WA latents conditioned on visual context and end-stage correction requirements, thereby producing refined action chunks. We validate HALO-WA on four real-world precision manipulation tasks, where it improves the average success rate from 26.4\% for WA-base to 87.1\%, outperforming the strongest baseline by 19.2 percentage points while requiring only 45--75 minutes of online training per task. To facilitate reproducibility, we further conduct supplementary simulation experiments in RoboTwin and release the code at https://github.com/YeanRoot/HALO-WA.

</details>


### [55] [GPU-Accelerated Polygonal Signed Distance Functions for Real-Time Collision Avoidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04310)
*Taekwon Ga,Jongeun Choi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出多边形有符号距离函数(PSDF)，一种面向凸多边形机器人足迹与障碍物边界的精确几何距离计算方法，通过无权重、无分支的张量化GPU流水线实现批量计算与自动微分，并将其嵌入MPC中，实现高实时性、高保真的局部避障规划与控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 优化类局部规划中，碰撞避免约束在密集障碍物环境中计算量巨大，成为控制周期的瓶颈。现有方法难以同时兼顾计算效率与几何精度，亟需一种既精确又高效、可并行化的碰撞约束表示。

Method: 提出PSDF：一种基于凸多边形机器人足迹与障碍物边界边的精确有符号距离函数。实现为无权重、无分支的张量化几何流水线，支持GPU批量执行与自动微分。将PSDF嵌入模型预测控制，在基于序列二次规划的实时迭代框架中对阶段安全约束进行局部线性化，形成PSDF-MPC。架构上采用CPU/GPU分离：GPU批量计算PSDF值及梯度，CPU求解规模仅依赖系统维度和预测时长的稀疏二次规划问题。

Result: 微基准测试表明PSDF在可扩展性上优于有符号距离查询基线。闭环仿真与真实世界导航实验（含与优化类基线方法的对比）显示，PSDF-MPC在密集多边形环境中保持了实时可行性和鲁棒的碰撞避免能力。

Conclusion: PSDF-MPC成功将几何精确的碰撞约束高效嵌入实时MPC框架，通过GPU并行化与CPU/GPU计算分离，在密集障碍物场景中实现了实时性与避障鲁棒性的兼顾，验证了该方法在仿真与真实环境中的有效性。

Abstract: Optimization-based local planning and control require high-rate collision-avoidance constraint evaluation over a prediction horizon. In obstacle-dense environments, where feasible space is limited and the constraints become increasingly complex, the computational workload often dominates the control-cycle runtime. The resulting bottleneck motivates collision-avoidance constraints that combine computational efficiency with geometric fidelity. The proposed Polygonal Signed Distance Function (PSDF) is a geometry-exact signed distance function between a convex polygonal robot footprint and obstacles represented by their boundary edges. It is implemented as a weight-free, branch-free tensorized geometric pipeline enabling batched GPU execution and automatic differentiation. The PSDF is embedded into model predictive control by locally linearizing the stage-wise safety constraints within a sequential quadratic programming-based real-time iteration scheme, yielding the PSDF-embedded model predictive controller (PSDF-MPC). The design separates CPU/GPU computation so that the GPU evaluates batched PSDF values and gradients while the CPU solves a sparse quadratic program whose dimension is determined by system dimensions and horizon length, not by obstacle features. Microbenchmarks show that PSDF scales favorably against signed-distance query baselines. Closed-loop simulated and real-world navigation experiments, including comparisons with optimization-based baselines, demonstrate that PSDF-MPC maintains real-time feasibility and robust collision avoidance in dense polygonal environments.

</details>

Abstract: Evaluating autonomous driving systems in closed-loop settings requires realistic and interactive simulation, yet existing simulators largely rely on log replay or rule-based agents, limiting behavioral diversity and long-tail coverage. We propose an agent-driven simulation framework in which surrounding road participants are controlled by instruction-following large language models through a structured action interface, enabling intentional and reactive behaviors while preserving physical plausibility. Furthermore, we introduce SemanticPlan, a benchmark of closed-loop planning in long-tail and semantically rich scenarios that augment real nuPlan scenes with multiple interactive agents following diverse language instructions. In this paper, we introduce surgical affordance prediction, which identifies actionable regions for fundamental surgical actions from visual data. Specifically, a novel adaptive feature fusion framework is proposed that leverages the complementary strengths of a self-supervised vision transformer encoder for its superior semantic understanding and a large-scale generative model encoder for its spatially-aware capability. Furthermore, we introduce a hierarchical prompt learning mechanism to adapt to varying procedural contexts. Finally, a scene-guided attention decoder is proposed to focus on critical surgical areas while suppressing background distractions. To validate the effectiveness, we established a new dataset, derived from publicly available surgical datasets with affordance annotations for three basic surgical actions: aspiration, clipping, and retraction. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance. Moreover, we validate our framework's applicability for downstream automation on a realistic lung and prostate phantom, and results show that the predicted affordance maps successfully enable autonomous surgical actions.

### [59] [ACE-Brain-0.5: A Unified Embodied Foundational Model for Physical Agentic AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04426)
*ACE-Brain Team,:,Ziyang Gong,Haoming Gu,Zehang Luo,Tianyi Zhang,Tao Tao,Yixiao Chi,Zhe Liu,Lingsi Zhu,Jingyuan Liu,Anke Tang,Songze Li,Yilun Kong,Ningjing Liu,Tianyu Zhu,Yunpeng Qing,Shuang Luo,Xiang Liu,Shi Fu,Dawei Nie,Sixiang Liu,Zhexi Wen,Feng Pan,Xiaofeng Wang,Zhi Hou,Chunxiao Liu,Xue Yang,Junchi Yan,Hengshuang Zhao,Dacheng Tao,Xiaogang Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: ACE-Brain-0.5 是一个统一的具身基础模型，将机器人智能组织为空间感知、决策制定、具身交互、自我监控和自我改进五个耦合功能，在单个8B骨干网络上实现闭环，并通过SSR+训练策略避免跨任务干扰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身AI系统存在碎片化问题：端到端策略缺乏空间推理与规划能力，而机器人-智能体系统虽能编排工具但无法学习共享表征。这种割裂限制了通用物理智能体AI的发展。

Method: 基于ACE-Brain-0（以空间智能为共享脚手架），将其扩展为闭环基础模型。单一8B骨干网络同时实例化空间感知、决策、交互、自我监控四项功能；提出SSR+训练策略（在Scaffold-Specialize-Reconcile基础上加入Reactivate阶段）以统一多能力而不产生跨任务干扰；第五项功能（自我改进）通过一个伴随框架从rollout中更新任务模式、空间记忆和失败恢复案例等外部执行状态来实现。

Result: 在15个基准测试中，ACE-Brain-0.5在18项空间感知与定位基准中的14项上超越ACE-Brain-0，取得有竞争力的导航与操作性能，并在分布内（ID）和分布外（OOD）设置下提供强健的进度估计。

Conclusion: ACE-Brain-0.5 标志着向通用物理智能体AI迈出的早期一步。

Abstract: Embodied AI is moving from isolated perception or action modules toward physical agents that understand, plan under goals, act through robot bodies, monitor progress, and improve from experience. Existing systems address this loop only in parts: end-to-end policies generate actions but often lack spatial reasoning, planning, and execution assessment, while robot-agent systems orchestrate tools or specialists but do not learn a shared representation. This fragmentation limits general Physical Agentic AI. We present ACE-Brain-0.5, a unified embodied foundation model that organizes robot intelligence into five coupled functions: spatial perception, decision making, embodied interaction, self-monitoring, and self-improvement. Built on ACE-Brain-0, which established spatial intelligence as a shared scaffold across robot platforms, ACE-Brain-0.5 extends an understanding-centric model into a closed-loop foundation model. A single 8B backbone instantiates the first four functions: grounding objects and affordances, reasoning over 3D and egocentric spatial relations, decomposing instructions into subgoals, generating navigation and manipulation actions, and estimating progress for verification and recovery. To unify these capabilities without cross-task interference, we introduce SSR+, which extends Scaffold-Specialize-Reconcile with a Reactivate stage after task-vector merging. The fifth function, self-improvement, is realized by a companion framework that updates external execution state, including task schemas, spatial memory, and failure-recovery cases, from rollouts. Across fifteen benchmarks, ACE-Brain-0.5 improves over ACE-Brain-0 on 14 of 18 spatial perception and grounding benchmarks, achieves competitive navigation and manipulation performance, and provides strong progress estimation in ID and OOD settings. Together, these results mark an early step toward general Physical Agentic AI.

### [60] [RoboDojo: A Unified Sim-and-Real Benchmark for Comprehensive Evaluation of Generalist Robot Manipulation Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04434)
*Tianxing Chen,Yue Chen,Zixuan Li,Junyuan Tang,Kailun Su,Weijie Wan,Baijun Chen,Haoran Lu,Haowen Yan,Honghao Su,Zhiyang Dou,Kaixuan Wang,Dandan Zhang,Yunze Liu,Yan Qin,Qiwei Liang,Qiwei Wu,Zijian Lin,Wenwei Lin,Yuran Wang,Minghua He,Tianshu Wu,Ruihai Wu,Jingquan Zhou,Kai-Chong Lei,Haibao Yu,Yuanfeng Ji,Weiyang Jin,Guanyu Lin,Xiaofan Li,Qi Xiong,Renjing Xu,Zhongyu Li,Wenhao Chai,Enze Xie,Ziwei Wang,Yao Mu,Hao Dong,Wojciech Matusik,Mingyu Ding,Wenbo Ding,Ping Luo,Masayoshi Tomizuka*

TL;DR: RoboDojo 是一个统一的仿真与真实世界机器人操作基准，包含 42 个仿真任务和 18 个真实任务，覆盖五种能力维度，并通过 XPolicyLab 支持 30 种策略的一体化评估，建立了公开排行榜。


<details>

Method: 提出 RoboDojo 基准，包含 42 个仿真任务与 18 个真实世界任务。仿真基准评估五个维度：泛化能力、记忆能力、精度、长视距执行和开放词汇指令遵循；真实基准将策略暴露于具有挑战性的物理部署条件。通过 Isaac Sim 中的异构并行仿真实现可扩展评估，并构建 RoboDojo-RealEval 真实世界评估系统，提供远程云访问、标准化硬件、场景重置、评估协议和部署接口。借助 XPolicyLab 平台，策略可一次性集成并在仿真与真实环境中以最小适配进行评估。

Result: 在 XPolicyLab 中集成了 30 种策略并在 RoboDojo 上完成评估，建立了公开排行榜，提供了当前策略性能的系统性分析。

Conclusion: RoboDojo 作为一个统一仿真与真实的综合基准，显著提升了对通用机器人操作策略能力的评估广度和深度，为社区提供了标准化、可复现且可扩展的评估平台，并通过对 30 种策略的系统分析揭示了当前方法的优势与不足。

Abstract: Generalist robot manipulation policies have advanced rapidly, yet existing benchmarks remain limited in systematically evaluating their capabilities. Many rely on simple, short-horizon, or skill-narrow tasks with limited capability coverage, and are often conducted only in simulation or only in the real world. Simulation enables scalable feedback but misses physical deployment challenges, while real-world evaluation is costly, time-consuming, and difficult to reproduce. We introduce RoboDojo, a unified sim-and-real benchmark for comprehensive evaluation of generalist robot manipulation policies. RoboDojo includes 42 simulation tasks and 18 real-world tasks covering diverse and complementary manipulation capabilities. The simulation benchmark evaluates five dimensions: generalization, memory, precision, long-horizon execution, and open-vocabulary instruction following, while the real-world benchmark exposes policies to challenging physical-world deployment conditions. RoboDojo supports scalable evaluation through heterogeneous parallel simulation in Isaac Sim and provides RoboDojo-RealEval, a reproducible real-world evaluation system with remote cloud access, standardized hardware, scene reset, evaluation protocol, and deployment interface. Together with XPolicyLab, policies can be integrated once and evaluated across simulation and real-world settings with minimal adaptation. We integrate 30 policies into XPolicyLab and evaluate them on RoboDojo, establishing a public leaderboard and systematic analysis of current policy performance. The website is available at http://robodojo-benchmark.com/.

Method: 提出基于可达性分析的鲁棒性验证框架，并引入连续时间神经常微分方程（Neural ODE）分类模型，结合SilCam颗粒成像仪的高分辨率成像能力，对环境扰动下的模型鲁棒性进行形式化验证。

Result: 验证框架能够作为自动化过滤器，为模型在面对模糊数据时的稳定性提供形式化保证，有效提升了自主采样的可靠性。

Conclusion: 所提出的验证框架可有效提升浮游生物原位分类的鲁棒性，减少误分类，降低海洋生物学家的后处理工作负担，为自主水下航行器的持久监测提供了更可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: The assessment of planktonic standing stocks and microorganism structures is critical for understanding upper ocean biological processes. Currently, autonomous underwater vehicles (AUVs) equipped with in-situ optical imaging and artificial intelligence (AI) methods offer a promising solution for persistent surveillance, mapping and monitoring of planktonic life. However, current AI methods often lack robustness in dynamic, unstructured environments, where environmental noise and non-biological artifacts lead to frequent misclassifications. Standard convolutional neural network (CNN) classifiers often struggle with such conditions, leading to misclassifications that require time-consuming manual validation by marine biologists.
  To address this issue, we propose a novel robustness verification framework for in-situ plankton classifiers based on reachability analysis. We also introduce a continuous-time neural ordinary differential equation (neural ODE) classification model leveraging the high-resolution imaging capabilities of the SilCam particle imager. In this paper, we demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework by formally verifying the robustness of the neural ODE model against environmental perturbations. We demonstrate that our verification framework acts as an automated filter providing formal guarantees of model stability against ambiguous data, thereby improving the reliability of autonomous sampling and reducing the post-processing workload.

</details>


### [62] [Mask2Real-WM: Segmentation Masks as a Sim-to-Real Bridge for Controllable Dexterous World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04546)
*Riccardo O. Feingold,Davide Liconti,Chenyu Yang,Robert K. Katzschmann*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Mask2Real-WM 提出一种两阶段动作条件世界模型，通过将像素预测解耦为分割掩码的动力学模型和基于 ControlNet+Stable Video Diffusion 的渲染模型，在缩小仿真到真实差距的同时实现对 23 自由度灵巧操作的精确动作可控性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型在处理高维动作空间（如 23 自由度灵巧手）时，难以同时实现细粒度的逐关节动作可控性和逼真的像素级预测。仿真数据丰富但存在 sim-to-real 差距，真实数据稀缺且昂贵。本文旨在利用分割空间更小的域差距，使动力学模型能从大规模仿真预训练中受益，再通过少量真实数据微调来弥合这一鸿沟。

Method: 提出 Mask2Real-WM 两阶段架构：第一阶段为动力学模型，接收历史分割掩码与 23-DoF 动作序列，预测未来分割掩码，通过在 50+ 小时合成仿真数据上预训练、在不到 2.5 小时真实演示上微调来捕获精确的物体和手部运动；第二阶段为渲染模型，以 ControlNet 增强的 Stable Video Diffusion 为骨干，将预测的分割掩码映射为逼真 RGB 视频帧。

Result: 在灵巧拾放基准上的实验表明：(1) 掩码条件化和仿真预训练两者缺一不可，共同支撑全部 23 自由度的逐关节动作可控性；(2) 单体式基线方法虽能捕捉粗略的手部和末端执行器轨迹，但无法可靠反映细粒度的逐关节动作效果。

Conclusion: 通过在分割空间中建模动力学并利用大规模仿真预训练，Mask2Real-WM 实现了高自由度灵巧操作中精确的动作条件视频预测，为机器人策略评估、规划与数据增强提供了有效的世界模型方案。

Abstract: Action-conditioned world models allow robots to predict the future consequences of candidate actions without additional physical interaction, supporting policy evaluation, planning, and data augmentation. We present Mask2Real-WM, a two-stage action-conditioned world model for dexterous manipulation that decouples pixel prediction into a dynamics model and a rendering model. The dynamics model predicts future segmentation masks from past masks and 23-DoF action sequences. The rendering model maps the predicted masks to photorealistic RGB using a ControlNet-augmented Stable Video Diffusion backbone. The smaller sim-to-real gap in segmentation space enables the dynamics model to benefit from large-scale pretraining on over 50 h of synthetic simulation data, followed by fine-tuning on fewer than 2.5 h of real demonstrations. Experiments on a dexterous pick-and-place benchmark show that mask conditioning and simulation pretraining are both required for per-DoF action controllability across all 23 degrees of freedom. In contrast, monolithic baselines capture broad hand and end-effector trajectories but do not reliably reflect fine-grained, per-joint action effects.

</details>


### [63] [HUGS: Guiding Unified Dexterous Grasp Synthesis Across Modes and Scales via Learned Human Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04554)
*Mingrui Yu,Yongpeng Jiang,Yongyi Jia,Kangchen Lv,Li Huang,Yi Ren,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: HUGS 提出了一种基于人类先验引导的统一灵巧抓取合成框架，通过学习对象条件化的人类抓取先验来指导力闭合优化，能够跨尺度和接触模式（从双指捏取到双臂抓取）合成多样化且高质量的机器人抓取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有灵巧抓取合成方法依赖手工设计的期望接触和初始化启发式规则，难以在合成成功率和多样性之间取得平衡，尤其难以统一处理从双指到双臂、从小物体到大物体的多尺度多模式抓取。

Method: HUGS 首先在自采集的包含304个物体、1.8K次抓取的人类抓取数据集上训练一个对象条件化的人类先验模型，捕捉人类抓取偏好；在合成阶段，该先验自适应地提出接触模式和腕部初始化，指导力闭合感知的优化过程，从而统一处理不同尺度和接触模式。

Result: 利用 HUGS 在157K个场景上合成了3.2M个机器人抓取，覆盖物体半对角线长度从2 cm到30 cm，接触模式从双指到双臂。基于合成数据训练的模型在真实世界中能够自主选择合适接触模式，实现从螺丝到大型箱体的抓取。

Conclusion: HUGS 通过人类先验引导实现了统一、高成功率且多样化的灵巧抓取合成，证明了人类先验在跨模式跨尺度抓取中的有效性，并为机器人抓取的自主模式选择提供了数据基础。

Abstract: Dexterous grasping across diverse object scales requires contact modes ranging from two-finger pinches to bimanual grasps. Existing dexterous grasp synthesis methods reduce the high-dimensional optimization space with manually designed expected contacts and initialization heuristics, which struggle to balance synthesis success rate and diversity. We present HUGS (Human-prior-guided Unified Dexterous Grasp Synthesis), a human-prior-guided framework for unified dexterous grasp synthesis across modes and scales. Instead of directly retargeting human demonstrations, HUGS learns an object-conditioned human prior that captures human grasp preferences and guides downstream force-closure-aware optimization. The prior is trained on a compact self-collected human grasp dataset with 1.8K grasps over 304 objects, providing broad coverage of object scales and contact modes. During synthesis, HUGS adaptively proposes contact modes and wrist initializations, substantially improving the balance between contact-mode coverage and synthesis success rate over heuristic-based methods. With HUGS, we synthesize 3.2M robotic grasps over 157K scenes, spanning object half-diagonal lengths from 2 cm to 30 cm and modes from two-finger to bimanual grasps. Models trained on the synthesized dataset autonomously select appropriate contact modes in the real world, enabling grasping from screws to large boxes.

### [64] [Simple-to-Complex Structured Demonstrations for Vision-Language-Action Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04591)
*Xinchuan Qiu,Yi Yu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从简单到复杂的演示组织策略，用于VLA模型的模仿学习，通过任务分解、环境标准化和渐进式复杂度组织三个原则，在双臂机器人平台上验证了该方法在任务成功率和训练稳定性上优于传统的端到端完整轨迹收集基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA研究主要关注模型架构、训练策略和数据集规模，忽视了演示数据的收集与组织方式对模仿学习的影响。作者认为演示组织是模仿学习中一个基础但被忽略的关键因素，直接关系到策略学习效率、训练稳定性和泛化能力。

Method: 提出简单到复杂的结构化演示收集策略，包含三个原则：（i）将复杂操作任务分解为渐进可学习的子技能；（ii）标准化交互环境以减少不必要的变异性；（iii）按照任务复杂度递增的方式组织演示。使VLA模型先掌握基础操作技能，再学习复杂任务组合。

Result: 在方块抓取与分类、毛巾折叠两个代表性任务上评估，实验结果表明，相比直接收集端到端完整轨迹的基线方法，该方法在任务成功率和训练稳定性上均有一致性提升。

Conclusion: 演示组织是VLA学习中此前未被充分探索但重要的因素，该研究为高效技能获取、可扩展数据集构建和长时序机器人操作提供了实用洞见。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have demonstrated strong capabilities in robotic manipulation by integrating visual perception, language understanding, and robot action generation. Existing research has primarily focused on improving model architectures, training strategies, and dataset scale, while little attention has been paid to how demonstrations are collected and organized. We identify demonstration organization as a fundamental yet overlooked aspect of imitation learning, as it directly affects policy learning efficiency, training stability, and policy generalization. To address this gap, we propose a simple-to-complex structured demonstration collection strategy for VLA learning using a dual-arm robotic platform. Our approach systematically organizes data through three general principles: (i) decomposing complex manipulation tasks into progressively learnable sub-skills, (ii) standardizing the interaction environment to reduce unnecessary variability, and (iii) organizing demonstrations according to progressively increasing task complexity. This structured design enables VLA models to first acquire fundamental manipulation skills before learning increasingly complex task compositions, facilitating more effective learning of long-horizon manipulation tasks. We evaluate the proposed strategy on two representative robotic manipulation tasks: block grasping and sorting, and towel folding. Experimental results show consistent improvements in task success rate and training stability compared with the baseline method of directly collecting end-to-end complete task trajectories. These findings highlight demonstration organization as a previously underexplored but important factor in VLA learning and provide practical insights into efficient skill acquisition, scalable dataset construction, and long-horizon robotic manipulation.

### [65] [SEAM: Smooth Execution of Action-Chunked Motion for Vision-Language-Action Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04609)
*Dijia Zhan,Xuemiao Xu,Jinyi Li,Jie Tang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: SEAM 是一种无需训练的推理时方法，针对流匹配 VLA 策略中固定长度动作块之间的多模态分叉问题，利用已执行前缀的未执行尾部作为一致性参考，通过速度引导损失 steering（VLS）在每个欧拉步骤后进行闭式修正，从而平滑块边界过渡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 VLA 策略执行固定长度动作块时存在多模态分叉问题：相邻块由独立高斯潜变量生成，可能收敛到不兼容的轨迹模式，在块边界产生突变不连续。现有解决方案（需反向传播、拒绝采样或重训练）在计算成本或任务可靠性上均有折损，亟需一种低开销且无需训练的平滑方案。

Method: 提出 SEAM，核心机制为速度引导损失 steering（VLS）：(1) 利用同步执行洞察——机器人在消耗已执行前缀后，前一块的未执行尾部可作为解析一致性参考；(2) 从该尾部导出时间依赖的目标；(3) 在每个欧拉步骤后施加闭式修正，无需通过策略网络进行反向传播。整个过程为推理时、无训练、流匹配框架。

Result: 在 LIBERO-10 基准上使用 pi_0.5 策略，SEAM 将边界 jerk 降低 28%，块过渡不连续性降低 27%，保持与基线相当的任务成功率，且去噪循环开销接近无引导基线。

Conclusion: SEAM 证明通过推理时、无训练的闭式修正即可有效平滑 VLA 动作块边界，在保持任务性能的同时显著降低过渡不连续性，是一种轻量且实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies that execute fixed-length action chunks can exhibit multimodal bifurcation: a cross-chunk inconsistency in which adjacent chunks generated from independent Gaussian latents can converge to incompatible trajectory modes, producing abrupt discontinuities at chunk boundaries. Existing remedies either require backpropagation through the policy at each denoising step, rely on rejection sampling, or require retraining, each trading computational cost or task reliability for smoother transitions. We propose SEAM (Smooth Execution of Action-Chunked Motion), a training-free inference-time method for flow matching VLAs. SEAM exploits a simple synchronous-execution insight: after the robot consumes the executed prefix, the previous chunk's unexecuted tail is already available as an analytic consistency reference. Its core mechanism, Velocity-guided Loss Steering (VLS), derives a time-dependent target from this tail and applies a closed-form correction after each Euler step without backpropagating through the policy network. On LIBERO-10 with pi_0.5, SEAM reduces boundary jerk by 28%, reduces chunk transition discontinuity by 27%, preserves baseline-level task success, and keeps denoising-loop cost near the unguided baseline.

</details>


### [66] [RoboVista: Evaluating Vision Language Models for Diverse Robot Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04610)
*Shuangyu Xie,Kaiyuan Chen,Ziyang Chen,Simeon Adebola,Yixuan Huang,Zehan Ma,Tianshuang Qiu,Wentao Yuan,Dhruv Shah,Pannag R. Sanketi,Ken Goldberg*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出 Robot Question Answering (RQA) 模块化评估框架和 RoboVista 基准，通过 474 个视觉问答实例、覆盖 39 种任务类型来评估 VLM 在机器人推理中的决策能力，发现当前 VLM 存在显著不足且基准性能与真实任务执行高度相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人应用（工业、农业等）需在不同形态、视觉条件和规划复杂性下运行。VLM 虽有潜力作为通用机器人推理基础，但现有基准多基于遥操作端到端数据集，缺乏对机器人行为底层决策组件的模块化理解，无法有效评估 VLM 与多样化机器人任务的对齐程度。

Method: 提出 Robot Question Answering (RQA) 模块化评估框架，并构建 RoboVista 基准——从真实机器人系统、研究论文和专家标注中策展，包含 474 个 VQA 实例及人工标注的推理过程，覆盖农业、工业、家庭、手术机器人、自动驾驶和开放机器人数据集共 39 种任务类型。同时进行物理机器人实验验证基准与真实任务表现的关联性。

Result: 在 RoboVista 上的实验表明，当前最先进的 VLM 在机器人推理任务上存在显著性能差距。物理机器人实验进一步表明，RoboVista 基准上的表现与真实世界任务执行效果之间存在强相关性。

Conclusion: RQA 框架和 RoboVista 基准为评估 VLM 的机器人推理能力提供了结构化、模块化的方法，揭示了现有模型的不足，并为未来通用机器人推理研究指明了方向。

Abstract: Diverse applications for robotics, such as industry and agriculture, require robots to operate across various embodiments, changing visual conditions, and complex planning. Vision-Language Models (VLMs) offer a promising foundation for general-purpose and interpretable robotic reasoning. Aligning VLMs with diverse robot applications requires a modular understanding of the individual decision components that underlie robotic behavior. Capturing such structure is challenging for conventional robot benchmarks that are primarily based on teleoperated, end-to-end datasets. We propose Robot Question Answering (RQA), a modular evaluation framework and RoboVista, a benchmark curated from real robotic systems, research papers, and expert annotations. RoboVista contains 474 Visual Question Answering (VQA) instances with human annotated reasoning and covers 39 unique task types in agricultural, industrial, domestic, surgical robotics, autonomous driving, and open robot datasets. Experiments on RoboVista show that state-of-the-art VLMs exhibit substantial gaps. Physical robot experiments suggest strong correlation between RoboVista performance and real-world task execution.

*Kyungmin Jung,Angad Bajwa,Junha Yoo,Arturo Del Castillo Bernal,James Richard Forbes*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出基于高斯过程的连续时间轨迹估计框架，融合多普勒测速仪(DVL)、立体相机和IMU的异步测量数据；设计了基于学习的特征提取与匹配的视觉前端，增强对水下环境的鲁棒性；框架支持无缝集成额外传感器模态，且无需重新配置即可适应不同环境。

Conclusion: 所提出的连续时间多传感器融合框架有效解决了水下环境中的定位与建图难题，基于学习的视觉前端显著提升了鲁棒性，且系统具备良好的扩展性和环境适应性。

Abstract: This paper presents a novel acoustic-visual-inertial odometry solution leveraging a continuous-time trajectory estimation framework for unmanned underwater vehicles. Underwater environments present unique challenges for visual localization and mapping, such as light attenuation, illumination variance, and the presence of particulate matter. This motivates the use of additional sensing modalities and a visual tracking pipeline that is robust to diverse subsea conditions. The proposed system is the first continuous-time trajectory estimation framework based on Gaussian processes to fuse asynchronous measurements from a Doppler velocity log, a stereo camera, and an inertial measurement unit. Additionally, a novel visual frontend is proposed, incorporating learning-based feature extraction and matching that is robust to the specific challenges that subsea environments present. The proposed framework enables seamless integration of additional sensor modalities in continuous-time and is adaptable to different environments without reconfiguration. The proposed system is extensively tested on real-world underwater inspection datasets, where it outperforms state-of-the-art visual-inertial and acoustic-visual-inertial SLAM algorithms in accuracy, robustness, and trajectory coverage. Notably, the proposed system outperforms the state-of-the-art despite only forming short-term visual data associations.

### [68] [SILO: Simulation-in-the-Loop Sim-to-Real Transfer for Multi-Stage Cable Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04616)
*Stone Tao,Jie Xu,Hesam Rabeti,Yashraj Narang,Yijie Guo,Iretiayo Akinola*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种用于多阶段线缆布线的sim-to-real强化学习框架，利用GPU并行仿真训练可泛化的操控策略，并通过SILO执行框架、局部化RL策略和鲁棒状态估计实现从仿真到现实的成功迁移，在实际任务中相比现有方法成功率更高、周期时间减半。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性可变形物体（如线缆、绳索）的操控因复杂变形而极具挑战。现有数据驱动方法（尤其是模仿学习）虽然在受限场景下有所成效，但通常需要针对特定任务和线缆类型采集数千次演示，可扩展性和泛化能力严重受限。因此需要一种更高效、泛化能力更强的解决方案。

Method: 提出一个sim-to-real强化学习框架用于多阶段线缆布线：1）利用GPU并行化仿真近似线性可变形行为，在数千个并行仿真环境中训练策略，使其泛化到多样化的线缆几何形状和变形模式；2）提出结合SILO（Simulation In the LOop）执行框架、局部化RL策略和鲁棒线缆状态估计的部署策略，以弥合sim-to-real差距。

Result: 在真实世界的线缆布线任务中，该方法相比先前最先进的学习方法取得了更高的成功率，并且周期时间缩短了2倍。据作者所知，这是首次在多阶段线缆布线中成功实现RL策略的sim-to-real迁移。

Conclusion: GPU并行仿真结合SILO执行框架、局部化策略和鲁棒状态估计，能够有效实现多阶段线缆布线的sim-to-real迁移，在真实任务中显著优于现有方法，为该领域开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Linear-deformable manipulation remains challenging due to the complex deformations of objects such as cables and ropes. Prior data-driven approaches, particularly imitation learning, have shown some promise in narrowly defined settings but typically require thousands of demonstrations for specific tasks and cable types, limiting scalability and generalization. We introduce a sim-to-real reinforcement learning (RL) framework for multi-stage cable routing that leverages GPU-parallelized simulation to approximate linear deformable behaviors. Training across thousands of parallel simulations enables the learned policies to generalize across diverse cable geometries and deformation patterns. To bridge the sim-to-real gap, we propose a novel deployment strategy that combines a Simulation In the LOop (SILO) execution framework, localized RL policies, and robust cable state estimation. On real-world cable routing tasks, our approach achieves higher success rates and 2x reduction in cycle times compared to prior state-of-the-art learning methods. To our knowledge, this is the first successful sim-to-real transfer of RL policies for multi-stage cable routing. Videos and additional visualizations are available at https://silo-cable-routing.github.io/

</details>

### [69] [iFLYTEK-Embodied-Omni Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02542)
*Yuan Zhang,Jingfei Ni,Guanchen Lu,Shiqi Zhang,Qingshan Xu,Chi Liu,Xin Nie,Wenjie Xu,Lin Gao,Zhiyuan Cheng,Mingxin Zhou,Jiajia Wu,Diyuan Liu,Jia Pan,Chao Ji*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: iFLYTEK-Embodied-Omni 是一个统一的多模态基础模型，将视觉-语言理解、视频生成和动作生成整合到单一Omni框架中，通过"大脑-小脑"协作架构实现从指令理解到可执行动作的端到端映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身智能方法通常将视觉-语言推理、世界建模和动作生成分开处理，级联流水线先合成未来观测再推断动作会引入接口瓶颈和累积预测误差。需要一个统一模型来联合建模视觉、语言和动作，消除这些局限性。

Method: 提出iFLYTEK-Embodied-Omni，包含三个组件：视觉-语言模型(VLM)和视频生成模型(VGM)构成"大脑"，负责指令理解、任务规划、进度跟踪和未来视觉状态预测；动作生成模型(AGM)作为"小脑"，将规划的子目标和共享多模态上下文转换为可执行动作块。各组件通过共享多模态自注意力机制通信。训练方面：(1)构建包含动作标注/无动作标注的具身视频、具身推理、具身感知和通用图文数据的综合数据集；(2)采用四阶段策略，逐步训练VLM、VGM、AGM，最后联合微调完整模型。

Result: 该模型在一个统一框架内同时实现了多模态指令理解、未来视觉状态预测和精确动作生成，通过大脑-小脑协作消除了级联流水线的接口瓶颈和复合预测误差。

Conclusion: iFLYTEK-Embodied-Omni 验证了将视觉-语言理解、视频生成和动作生成统一到一个Omni框架中的可行性，大脑-小脑协作架构为通用具身智能体提供了一种端到端、无级联瓶颈的解决方案。

Abstract: General-purpose embodied agents must understand multimodal instructions, anticipate how their environment will evolve, and produce precise control actions over extended horizons. Existing approaches typically specialize in visual-language reasoning, video-based world modeling, or action generation, while cascaded pipelines that first synthesize future observations and then infer actions can introduce interface bottlenecks and compound prediction errors. We present iFLYTEK-Embodied-Omni, a unified multimodal foundation model that jointly models vision(videos and images), language, and action within a single Omni framework. Its modality-specific visual-language, video-generation, and action-generation components communicate through shared multimodal self-attention. This design establishes brain-cerebellum collaboration: the vision-language modeland video generation model form a high-level brain for instruction understanding, task planning, progress tracking, and future visual-state prediction, whereas the action generation modelserves as a low-level cerebellum that directly converts planned subgoals and shared multimodal context into executable action chunks. To develop these capabilities, we combine action-annotated and action-free embodied videos from human demonstrations and robot interactions with embodied reasoning, embodied perception, and general-purpose image-text data to construct a comprehensive dataset. We further adopt a four-stage strategy that progressively trains the VLM, VGM, and AGM before jointly fine-tuning the complete model.

</details>


### [70] [Internal Pluralism and the Limits of Pairwise Comparisons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02672)
*Bailey Flanigan,Michelle Si*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了在参与式设计或对齐中，强制性的局部成对比较可能因个体的内在多元主义（internal pluralism）而失效，表现为全局性偏好无法被局部捕捉以及强优先级冲突导致的行为扭曲；作者提出允许报告"犹豫不决"可显著减少学习偏好所需的查询量，并倡导直接引出多元优先级的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在参与式设计和AI对齐等场景中，局部成对比较被广泛用于学习人们对决策规则的偏好，但这一方法隐含两个强假设：（1）局部比较足以推断人们对全局决策规则的偏好；（2）人们总能果断回答这些比较。本文质疑当个体本身持有多种相互竞争的权威性优先级（即"内在多元主义"）时，这两个假设可能不成立，从而动机在于揭示和解决由此产生的偏好学习失效问题。

Method: 作者首先构建了一个形式化模型，用于刻画个体在内在多元主义下对决策规则的偏好——即个体依据多个权威性优先级（如比例性、平等主义、平等对待等）来评估决策规则。基于该模型，作者识别出强制性局部成对比较数据的两类失败模式：一是某些优先级具有本质上的全局性，局部比较无法捕捉其跨情境的依赖关系；二是即使优先级可用局部方式表达，强烈的优先级冲突也会导致内部冲突和行为扭曲。进一步，作者利用该模型探讨了允许个体表达"犹豫不决"的替代方案，并分析其对查询效率的影响。

Result: 研究发现：（1）比例性、平等主义、平等对待等优先级是"固有全局性"的——在某一案例中的含义取决于其他案例的情况，因此局部成对比较无法准确捕捉这些偏好；（2）即使优先级可局部表示，强烈优先级之间的张力会引发内部冲突，在强制比较时产生代价高昂的行为扭曲；（3）允许参与者报告犹豫不决可以显著减少准确学习偏好所需的查询数量。最终，模型指向应直接引出这些优先级本身，而非依赖间接的局部比较。

Conclusion: 强制性局部成对比较在个体存在内在多元主义时存在根本性局限。本文提出的形式化模型不仅诊断了这些失效，还指明了改进方向：偏好学习方法应直接引出个体所持的多元优先级，而非依赖可能产生误导的局部选择数据。这样做不仅能获得更忠实的偏好表征，还能提升可解释性，让人们真正看重的东西得到更准确的体现。

Abstract: Local pairwise comparisons are a standard tool for learning how people want decision rules to work, e.g., in participatory design or alignment. However, their use builds in two strong assumptions: that local comparisons are sufficient evidence about how a person wants an automated decision rule to behave, and that people can always answer those comparisons decisively. We investigate how these assumptions may be compromised under internal pluralism: the idea that an individual evaluates decision rules according to multiple authoritative priorities about how the rule should behave. We provide a formal model of such pluralistic preferences over decision rules, which then lets us identify two distinct failures of forced local pairwise comparison data. First, priorities such as proportionality, egalitarianism, and equal treatment are inherently global: what they imply in one case can depend on what happens elsewhere, so local comparisons may fail to capture them. Second, even when priorities are representable locally, tension between strongly-held priorities can generate internal conflict, producing potentially costly behavioral distortions when comparisons are forced. We then use our model to investigate the alternative -- allowing people to report indecision -- and our findings suggest that doing so can considerably reduce the number of queries needed to learn preferences accurately. We conclude by describing how our model points toward preference-learning methods that elicit these priorities directly, yielding more faithful and interpretable accounts of what people value.

</details>


### [71] [ASK in the Dark: Uncertainty-Gated LLM Assistance under Partial Observability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02686)
*Juarez Monteiro,Nathan Gavenski,Guilherme Lima,Francisco Galuppo,Odinaldo Rodrigues,Adriano Veloso*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对强化学习中部分可观测环境下的SLM引导问题，本文发现传统方法因缺乏上下文导致SLM几乎不贡献独立动作，提出ASK+通过轨迹感知上下文和结构化思维链将SLM从被动冗余检查转变为主动顾问，显著提升多项任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在POMDP设置下，现有vanilla uncertainty-gated方法几乎从不触发SLM的独立动作（overwrite rate接近零），作者将其归因于贫乏的自我中心prompt无法提供足够推理上下文，这是一个"上下文问题"而非"能力问题"。

Method: 提出ASK+方法：(1) 为SLM提供轨迹感知上下文，包括部分揭示的地图、访问位置和动作历史；(2) 引入结构化思维链推理；(3) 采用预测熵信号进行选择性查询，并论证该信号测量的是动作不确定性而非状态不确定性，在POMDP中仍有效。

Result: DoorKey任务：ASK+达93%成功率（vanilla ASK和PPO均为89%）；FourRooms：成功率从53%提升至70%；HigherLower：准确率达73.7%，匹配SLM-only上界。Qwen3.5-2B匹配或超越Qwen3.5-4B，证明prompt设计和选择性门控比模型规模更关键。

Conclusion: 通过将SLM从缺乏上下文的被动验证者转变为具有轨迹感知和结构化推理的主动顾问，ASK+显著提升了POMDP中的RL性能，且预测熵在部分可观测环境中仍然有效，小模型配合良好prompt设计即可实现有效引导。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning agents operating under partial observability must act on incomplete information, making them natural candidates for guidance from small language models (SLMs) that carry broad reasoning priors. Yet integrating SLM guidance into this setting has proven difficult: across all test environments, vanilla uncertainty-gated approaches achieve an overwrite rate at or near zero, meaning the SLM almost never contributes an independent action. We trace this failure to the bare egocentric prompt, which provides insufficient context for genuine reasoning, and identify it as a context problem rather than a capacity problem. We propose ASK+, which supplies the SLM with trajectory-aware context (a partially revealed map, visited positions, and action history) and structured chain-of-thought reasoning, converting it from a passive redundancy check into a more informative consultant that occasionally corrects the policy. We further establish that the predictive entropy signal used for selective querying measures action uncertainty rather than state uncertainty and remains informative in POMDPs, making uncertainty-gated assistance viable beyond fully observable settings. The stateful prompt drives substantial gains: on DoorKey, where vanilla ASK matches PPO (both 89%), ASK+ reaches 93% success; on FourRooms, success climbs from 53% to 70%; on HigherLower, accuracy reaches 73.7%, matching the SLM-only upper bound. Across all environments, Qwen3.5-2B matches or exceeds Qwen3.5-4B, confirming that prompt design and selective gating dominate the impact of model scale, enabling guidance without large models.

</details>

*Sean R. Wilkinson,Valentine G. Anantharaj,Jong Youl Choi,Ketan Maheshwari,Marshall McDonnell,Massimiliano Lupo Pasini,Polina Shpilker,Renan Souza,Patrick Widener,Sarp Oral,Wesley Brewer*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领导级计算设施管理的大规模科学数据集在作为AI训练数据前通常需要大量转换，但现有框架未能将自动化转换、就绪度评估、溯源追踪和代理原生部署完全统一起来，存在明显的工具链断层。

Method: 提出REDI框架，核心为五阶段流水线架构（ingest→preprocess→transform→structure→output），每个阶段均配备溯源仪表化以实现可复现性，并支持作为代理可调用技能部署。配套工具SetGo自动处理FAIR合规性检查和目录发布。

Result: 在气候、蛋白质组学、材料科学和核聚变四个领域进行验证，所有数据集均成功从原始状态转换为AI就绪格式，输出经过领域专家参考标准验证。气候案例在Frontier超算上实现近理想的100节点并行扩展。溯源分析揭示文件I/O是流水线的主要成本，格式选择是一级优化杠杆。

Conclusion: REDI确立了跨领域科学AI自动化数据就绪平台的地位，将数据准备瓶颈转化为可复现、可复用的社区资产。

Abstract: Leadership computing facilities steward large-scale scientific datasets that routinely require substantial transformation before serving as AI training data. However, no existing framework fully unifies automated transformation, readiness assessment, provenance tracking, and agent-native deployment. We present REDI, an open-source framework that addresses this gap through a unified five-stage pipeline (ingest, preprocess, transform, structure, and output) with per-stage instrumentation for reproducibility and deployment as an agent-callable skill; companion tool SetGo automates FAIR compliance and catalog publication. Evaluated across climate, proteomics, materials science, and nuclear fusion, REDI transforms all datasets from raw to AI-ready, with outputs validated against domain-expert references, and preliminary results show near-ideal parallel scaling to 100 nodes on Frontier for the climate case. Provenance-instrumented profiling reveals file I/O as the dominant pipeline cost, with format selection a first-order optimization lever. These results establish REDI as a cross-domain platform providing automated data readiness for scientific AI, transforming data preparation bottlenecks into reproducible, reusable community assets.

### [73] [SwarmResearch: Orchestrating Coding Agents for Open-Ended Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02807)
*Yuvraj Virk,Zack Edds,Chunqiu Steven Xia,Lingming Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SwarmResearch 提出了一种编排器-子代理（orchestrator-subagent）架构，由一个 Shepherd Agent 利用全局上下文引导一组 Search Agent 在不同的 git 分支中独立探索，从而缓解长期运行编码代理过早收敛到单一方案的问题，在 13/15 个开放式优化任务上表现优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长期运行的编码代理（如 autoresearch）在开放式问题上倾向于过早收敛到单一高层方案，随后仅进行低层次编辑，错失其他更优解法。作者假设这一行为源于两个架构层面的设计缺陷：(1) 在单一长期运行的代理中累积上下文；(2) 仅暴露单一程序状态供编辑。

Method: 提出 SwarmResearch，采用编排器-子代理架构：一个 Shepherd Agent（牧羊代理）基于全局上下文进行高层决策与调度，引导一组 Search Agent（搜索代理）在各自独立的 git 分支中以局部上下文进行探索。通过在不同搜索深度自适应调整并行度，实现编排器引导的弹性扩展。

Result: 在开放式优化任务上，SwarmResearch 在 15 个任务中的 13 个上发现优于或媲美 SOTA 大模型引导进化及多代理技术的解，其优势来源于更高层次的探索。相比固定扩展的串行和并行代理，SwarmResearch 通过自适应并行度在不同搜索深度发现了性能更优的解。

Conclusion: SwarmResearch 验证了通过编排器-子代理架构解耦全局探索与局部利用，可以有效避免过早收敛，在开放式优化问题上取得更优结果，证明了自适应并行扩展策略的有效性。

Abstract: Long-running coding agents such as autoresearch can persistently discover optimizations for open-ended problems. However, they tend to converge onto a single high-level approach, then proceed with low-level edits while missing other superior approaches to the problem. We hypothesize two harness-level design choices contribute to this behavior: accumulating context in a single long-running agent and only exposing a single program state to edit. We introduce SwarmResearch, an orchestrator-subagent harness in which a Shepherd Agent uses global context to steer a population of Search Agents, each operating with local context in their respective git branch. On open-ended optimization tasks, SwarmResearch discovers better or comparable solutions to state-of-the-art LLM-guided evolution and multi-agent techniques on 13/15 tasks, driven by higher-level exploration. Compared with fixed scaling of serial and parallel agents, SwarmResearch's orchestrator-guided scaling discovers better-performing solutions by adapting parallelism at different search depths.

</details>


### [74] [Object-Centric Environment Modeling for Agentic Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02846)
*Yiyang Li,Tianyi Ma,Zehong Wang,Yijun Ma,Yanfang Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OCM 将智能体经验组织为可执行的对象中心环境模型，包含对象知识（Python类）和过程知识（可复用交互模式）两个代码库，通过在线反思-更新-验证循环维护，并在推理时采用渐进式知识披露，在基准测试中取得最优平均排名并减少无效动作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体的自由形式文本记忆随交互增长变得难以维护、验证和复用；现有符号化方法要么仅存储局部过程，要么假设过于简化的环境动态，缺乏结构化的、可执行的环境建模方案。

Method: OCM维护两个互联的代码库：对象知识（Python类定义环境实体与机制）和过程知识（记录可复用交互模式，须导入对象模型）。采用在线设置：每轮交互后反思轨迹，更新两个知识库，并验证所有过程在更新后的对象模型上可执行。推理时使用渐进式知识披露——先展示紧凑的代码签名，仅在需要时读取源码。

Result: OCM在多个基准测试中取得最优平均排名，并显著减少无效动作（invalid actions），验证了构建对象中心环境模型对智能体的益处。

Conclusion: 通过将经验结构化地组织为可执行的对象中心环境模型，LLM智能体能够更有效地积累和复用知识，OCM为此提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents can improve through accumulated experience, but free-form textual memories become difficult to maintain, validate, and reuse as interactions grow. Recent symbolic approaches learn executable skills or programmatic world models, yet often store local procedures or assume simplified dynamics. We propose Object-Centric Environment Modeling (OCM), which organizes experience into an executable object-centric environment model. OCM maintains two connected code bases: object knowledge, which defines environment entities and mechanisms as Python classes, and procedure knowledge, which records reusable interaction patterns that must import and use the object model. OCM works in an online setting: after each episode, OCM reflects on the trajectory, updates both knowledge bases, and verifies that all procedures execute against the updated object model. During future interaction, the agent uses progressive knowledge disclosure to inspect compact code signatures first and read source code only when needed. Experiments show that OCM achieves the best average rank across benchmarks and reduces invalid actions, demonstrating that agents can benefit from building object-centric environment models.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 构建MedCalc-Pro基准：收集2268例真实临床病例，覆盖14个科室的77种医学计算器，设计单计算器、多计算器、嵌套计算三种递进难度任务；2) 提出通用Agent框架：支持多工具选择和嵌套工具调用，利用结构化验证与证据审查机制抑制参数误差传播。

Conclusion: 该工作为在复杂医学计算场景中评估和应用LLM提供了新的基准与方法支撑，推动了医学计算领域向更真实临床情境的拓展。

Abstract: Current benchmarks for evaluating large language models (LLMs) in medical calculation are largely based on simplified settings, where each patient case corresponds to a single calculator and the required tool is explicitly specified in the query. However, real clinical scenarios often require multiple calculators for joint evaluation, nested-scale calculation, and fuzzy queries that do not directly specify the target calculator. To this end, we propose a new medical calculation benchmark, MedCalc-Pro, which covers three progressively challenging task settings: single-calculator, multi-calculator, and nested-calculator calculation settings. MedCalc-Pro contains 2,268 real-world clinical cases, covering 77 medical calculators across 14 clinical departments. Meanwhile, to address the limited performance of existing frameworks and methods in complex clinical scenarios, we further propose a more generalizable agent framework that supports multi-tool selection and nested-tool calling, while suppressing parameter error propagation through structured validation and evidence review. We conduct systematic comparisons across open-source, closed-source, and medical-specialized LLMs, and the results show that our framework achieves the best performance across all three task settings. This work provides a new benchmark and method for evaluating and applying LLMs in challenging medical calculation scenarios.

### [76] [Oyster-II: Reinforcement Learning for Constructive Safety Alignment in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02914)
*Jiyang Guan,Yong Xie,Jun Chen,Jiexi Liu,Zipeng Ye,Defeng Li,Jiayu Shen,Jialing Tao,Hui Xue*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Oyster-II 是一个基于强化学习的建设性安全对齐框架，采用 Zero-RL 范式和多阶段强化学习策略，解决了前代方法在分布外安全泛化不足和安全思维链过度泛化两大问题，在安全、有用性和可信度上全面超越了 Qwen3-14B 和 Oyster-I。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于拒绝的对齐策略虽然能减少有害内容生成，但会系统性拒绝合法用户需求。Oyster-I 提出的建设性安全范式虽有所改进，但其基于 SFT 的方案存在两个关键缺陷：(1) 对分布外场景的安全泛化能力不足；(2) 安全思维链过度泛化——安全推理模式被过度应用到良性查询上，损害了有用性和用户体验。

Method: 提出 Oyster-II，一个基于强化学习的建设性安全对齐框架。核心设计包括：采用 Zero-RL 范式（无需人工偏好标注的奖励信号），结合多阶段强化学习策略，在 SFT 基础上通过 RL 优化安全和有用性之间的平衡。

Result: 在广泛的基准测试上，Oyster-II 在安全维度全面超越了 Qwen3-14B 和前代 Oyster-I，达到了与 Qwen3-Max 和 Qwen3.5-397B 相当的跨规模性能。

Conclusion: 基于 RL 的建设性安全对齐是解决 LLM 安全与有用性权衡的有效路径。Zero-RL 结合多阶段 RL 策略能够显著缓解安全泛化不足和过度泛化问题，实现从拒绝到建设性回应的转变。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities across diverse applications, yet ensuring their simultaneous safety, helpfulness, and trustworthiness remains a persistent challenge. Conventional refusal-oriented alignment strategies mitigate harmful content generation but systematically fail to serve legitimate user needs, often withholding information that could safely and constructively address the underlying intent of sensitive queries. Building upon the constructive safety paradigm pioneered by Oyster-I, which moves beyond blanket refusal toward thoughtful, response-oriented safety alignment, we identify two critical limitations of its Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT)-based scheme: insufficient safety generalization to out-of-distribution scenarios and a phenomenon we term safety chain-of-thought (CoT) over-generalization, wherein safety-oriented reasoning patterns are excessively applied to benign queries, degrading helpfulness and user experience. To address these limitations, we propose Oyster-II, a reinforcement learning (RL)-based constructive safety alignment framework that adopts a Zero-RL paradigm combined with a multi-stage reinforcement learning strategy.Evaluated across extensive benchmarks, Oyster-II comprehensively surpasses both Qwen3-14B and its predecessor Oyster-I on safety dimensions, achieving cross-scale performance comparable to Qwen3-Max and Qwen3.5-397B.

</details>


### [77] [VERITAS: Towards a General-Purpose Replication Tool for Scientific Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02931)
*Haokun Liu,Filbert Aurelian Tjiaranata,Chenhao Tan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: VERITAS 是一个领域无关的论文复现框架，基于CLI编程智能体，能从论文和代码仓库中提取声明、自动运行实验并解决问题，最终给出复现评分和修复日志。在CORE-Bench和ReplicationBench两个基准上，覆盖计算机科学、社会科学、医学和天体物理学共65篇论文，VERITAS在各项指标上均达到最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI工具加速了科学出版，但同行评审和独立验证跟不上节奏。手动复现研究既慢又昂贵，而已有的自动化复现工作大多被封装为仅能在特定基准流水线中运行的配套智能体，缺乏通用复现工具。因此需要构建一个领域无关的通用复现框架。

Method: VERITAS围绕CLI编程智能体构建，输入论文、代码仓库或两者兼有。流程分三步：(1)从论文中提取所有声明（claims）；(2)运行论文的方法论，在此过程中自动检测并解决执行中出现的各类问题；(3)将实验运行的证据与每项声明进行比对判定。最终输出重要性加权的复现评分（Replication Score）、按严重程度分级的修复日志以及修复后的完整代码库。

Result: 在CORE-Bench和ReplicationBench两个基准上测试了65篇论文（涵盖计算机科学、社会科学、医学、天体物理学），VERITAS与两个基于相同模型和主机环境的强基线Claude Code相比，在所有指标上均取得领先，达到最先进水平。

Conclusion: VERITAS作为一个通用、领域无关的复现框架，有效填补了自动化科研复现领域的空白，在多个学科和基准上验证了其有效性和通用性，为加速科学验证提供了实用工具。

Abstract: AI tools are accelerating scientific publication while the systems that review it struggle to keep up, and independent verification of published research has become both harder and more important. As manual replication is slow and expensive, a growing line of work uses coding agents to automate parts of the process. Existing efforts are largely packaged as benchmarks with companion agents that only run inside the benchmark's own pipeline, and no general-purpose replication tool exists. We present VERITAS, a domain-agnostic replication framework built around CLI coding agents. Given a paper, a code repository, or both, VERITAS extracts the paper's claims, runs the methodology while resolving issues as they arise, and judges each claim against the evidence from experiment runs. The pipeline returns an importance-weighted Replication Score, a severity-rated log of every fix applied, and the patched codebase. We evaluate VERITAS on CORE-Bench and ReplicationBench, 65 papers spanning computer science, social science, medicine, and astrophysics. Against two strong Claude Code baselines on the same model and host environment, VERITAS achieves state-of-the-art performance and leads on every metric on both benchmarks.

### [78] [A Sliding-Window-Based Reinforcement Learning for Dynamic Assembly Flow Shop Scheduling with Multi-Product Delivery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02941)
*Junhao Qiu,Jianjun Liu,Ting Liu,Rongjie Liao,Zhantao Li,Qingfu Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对混合制造系统中多产品配套交付的在线调度难题，本文提出一种基于滑动窗口的强化学习框架（SWRL），通过滑动窗口过滤、时空图编码和动态动作映射等机制，在真实家电制造实例中实现了显著的拖期缩减和鲁棒性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多产品配套交付（kitting delivery）在集成加工与装配的混合制造系统中带来严峻的实时调度挑战：动态订单到达会同时改变供应依赖关系和可行的工件-机器分配集合。传统方法难以应对这种双重耦合动态性，且配套约束导致的尾产品瓶颈（tail-product bottleneck）会形成稀疏奖励景观，使常规深度强化学习方法难以有效训练。

Method: 首先将问题建模为基于异构图（heterogeneous graph）的马尔可夫决策过程，以刻画双层配套结构和尾产品瓶颈动态。在此基础上，SWRL框架包含三个核心组件：(1) 滑动窗口过滤机制，过滤非活跃节点并优先处理配套关键操作；(2) 时空图编码网络，追踪连续决策状态间的瓶颈转移；(3) 动态动作映射模块及约束等待策略，适应变拓扑下不断变化的动作空间。

Result: 在家电制造商的真实实例上进行实验，结果表明SWRL相较经典调度规则和现有深度强化学习方法实现了持续的拖期（tardiness）缩减，并在不同资源配置、订单负载和到达集中度下均展现出鲁棒性能。

Conclusion: SWRL框架通过滑动窗口过滤、时空图编码和动态动作映射三者协同，有效解决了柔性装配流水车间中多产品配套交付在线调度的稀疏奖励和变动作空间问题，在真实工业场景中验证了其有效性和鲁棒性，为混合制造系统的端到端在线调度提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Multi-product kitting delivery imposes significant challenges for real-time scheduling in hybrid manufacturing systems that integrate processing and assembly, as dynamic order arrivals simultaneously alter supply dependencies and the set of feasible job-machine assignments. This paper proposes a sliding-window-based reinforcement learning (SWRL) framework for end-to-end online scheduling in the flexible assembly flow shop scheduling problem with complex kitting constraints. The problem is formulated as a heterogeneous graph-based Markov decision process that captures the dual-layer kitting structure and the tail-product bottleneck dynamics that produce a sparse reward landscape. To address the resulting challenges, SWRL integrates a sliding-window filtering mechanism that filters inactive nodes and prioritizes kitting-critical operations, a spatiotemporal graph encoding network that tracks bottleneck shifts across consecutive decision states, and a dynamic action mapping module with a constrained waiting strategy that adapts to the changing action space under variable topologies. Experiments on real-world instances from a home appliance manufacturer demonstrate that SWRL achieves consistent tardiness reductions over classical dispatching rules and existing deep reinforcement learning methods, and exhibits robust performance across varying resource configurations, order loads, and arrival concentrations.

### [79] [Evaluating Generative Agents with Actions Grounded in Socially Distributed Task Environments using Incognita](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02975)
*Dan C. Hsu,Luke Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Incognita，一个用于评估语言智能体在"社会分布式任务环境"中表现的框架。该环境将任务知识分散在不同角色参与者之间，智能体必须通过社交沟通探索知识，通过接地气操作利用环境状态。实验显示，虽然更强的模型能获取更多隐藏知识并尝试更多操作，但整体可靠性仍然很低（最高成功率仅17.2%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试要么提供可执行动作和可验证结果（接地气基准），要么提供丰富的智能体交互（社交模拟环境），但两者缺乏结合。作者旨在填补这一空白，研究智能体如何在社会环境中同时进行知识探索（沟通）和状态利用（行动），即何时寻求知识、何时行动，以及行动是否被所获信息所证明。

Method: 提出 Incognita 框架，基于 Concordia 构建，将社交互动与接地气执行分离。智能体通过消息路由与用户或专家实体通信；专家实体中介可允许的操作；确定性子环境在规范状态上执行被接受的操作；离线评估器根据继承奖励对结果评分。具体实现 Incognita-Retail 将 tau-bench 零售场景转化为多实体环境，保留最终状态奖励语义。在18个按社交广度分层的任务上评估了三种生成式智能体模型，共540次试验。

Result: 三种模型成功率分别为0%、8.9%和17.2%；过早终止率从100%降至87%和58%。更强的模型能引出更多隐藏知识、接触更多实体、尝试更多接地气写入操作，但可靠性仍然较低。这些结果表明，社会分布式任务环境能在可靠成功之前暴露智能体的行为特征，包括知识引出、信息源选择、接地气行动尝试和过早完成信念等。

Conclusion: 社会分布式任务环境能够有效暴露语言智能体在可靠成功之前的关键行为模式。当前模型虽在逐步进步，但距离可靠部署仍有较大差距。该框架为研究智能体在社交-行动耦合场景中的能力提供了有价值的评估工具。

Abstract: Effective agency in social environments depends on when an agent seeks knowledge, when it acts, and whether its actions are justified by acquired information. Existing grounded benchmarks provide executable actions, persistent state, and verifiable outcomes, while social simulation environments provide rich interaction among language agents. We study an evaluation setting that combines these requirements. We define socially distributed task environments as interactive environments where task-relevant knowledge is partitioned across role-isolated participants and consequential actions are accessible only through them. Communication serves as exploration over role-partitioned knowledge, while grounded action serves as exploitation over environment state. We introduce Incognita, a Concordia-based framework that separates social interaction from grounded execution. The evaluated agent routes messages to a user or specialist entities; specialists mediate admissible operations; a deterministic sub-environment executes accepted operations over a canonical state; and an offline evaluator scores outcomes with inherited rewards. Incognita-Retail transforms tau-bench retail into a multi-entity environment while preserving final-state reward semantics. We evaluate three generative agent models on 18 tasks stratified by social breadth, with 540 trials. Progress appears in reward and behavior: success rises from 0 percent to 8.9 percent and 17.2 percent, while premature finalization falls from 100 percent to 87 percent and 58 percent. Stronger models elicit more hidden knowledge, contact more entities, and attempt more grounded writes, yet reliability remains low. These findings show that socially distributed task environments expose behavior before reliable success, including knowledge elicitation, source selection, grounded action attempts, and premature completion belief.

### [83] [Silicon Sampling via Cross-Survey Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03091)
*Chan-Tung Ku,Chan Hsu,Pei-Cing Huang,Frank Cheng-shan Liu,I-Ling Cheng,Yihuang Kang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出"跨调查迁移"（cross-survey transfer）这一更严格的评估框架，即给定受访者对一组问题的回答，让LLM预测同一调查中完全不同问题的答案。基于台湾选举与民主化研究（TEDS 2024）数据，作者发现零样本LLM在真正未见项目上达到52%准确率，接近监督学习的随机森林（差距仅6个百分点）；同时揭示了"构念可预测性层级"（党派态度67% → 主权议题23%）以及方差坍缩和安全对齐效应的微妙表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出跨调查迁移框架：给定受访者在TEDS 2024调查中一组问题的真实回答，要求LLM预测同一受访者在同一调查中另一组完全不同问题的答案。使用三款开源LLM（27B-120B参数），以监督机器学习模型（随机森林等）作为基线，进行个体层面的预测准确性比较。同时系统分析方差坍缩和安全对齐效应在不同模型家族中的表现。

Result: （1）零样本LLM在真正未见项目上达52%准确率，与使用同总体数据训练的监督随机森林差距仅6个百分点；（2）存在稳定的构念可预测性层级：党派态度预测准确率达67%，而对主权议题仅23%；（3）方差坍缩不仅影响LLM，也影响监督模型；安全对齐效应在不同模型家族间差异显著，比既往研究更为微妙。

Conclusion: 硅采样确实展现出替代传统调查研究的潜力，但其能力存在明确边界。跨调查迁移框架为评估LLM模拟人类受访者的真实预测能力提供了更严谨的方法，同时揭示了构念可预测性的结构差异以及方差坍缩、对齐效应等已知局限性的复杂本质。

Abstract: Silicon sampling-using large language models (LLMs) to simulate human survey respondents-has emerged as a promising approach for augmenting traditional survey research. However, most evaluations rely on distributional comparisons rather than individual-level prediction, which risks conflating pattern matching with coherent respondent-level prediction. We propose cross-survey transfer, a more rigorous evaluation framework in which an LLM is given a respondent's answers to one set of questions and must predict their answers to entirely different questions from the same survey. Using data from the Taiwan Election and Democratization Study (TEDS) 2024, three open-weight LLMs (27B-120B parameters), and supervised machine learning baselines, we find that: (1) zero-shot LLMs achieve 52% accuracy on genuinely unseen items, closing to within 6 percentage points (pp) of a supervised random forest trained on same-population data; (2) a stable construct predictability hierarchy emerges, from 67% for partisan attitudes to 23% for sovereignty; and (3) variance collapse and safety alignment effects-two commonly cited LLM limitations-turn out to be more nuanced than previously reported, with variance collapse affecting supervised models as well and alignment effects varying dramatically across model families. These findings clarify both the promise and boundaries of silicon sampling.

### [84] [APeB: Benchmarking Personalization Ability of Large Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03162)
*Garry Yang,Zizhe Chen,Xinru Chen,Yongqiang Chen,Jianxiang Wang,Deyu Zou,Linyi Ding,Jialiang Wu,Yunzhong He,Yu Gong,James Cheng,Huaixiao Tou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出个性化产品搜索（PPS）测试平台APeB，评估LLM智能体在原始模糊查询下的个性化能力。研究发现现有模型在处理需推断隐含意图的早期查询时表现不佳，主要归因于历史利用不足；所提出的VQRA查询精炼管线通过改进历史使用实现了稳定提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体在用户发出原始、欠指定查询时难以实现个性化，因为智能体需要推断隐含意图、从噪声交互历史中提取偏好并在多个候选项中做出选择。然而，现有基准测试通常依赖用户精炼后的查询或简化的历史记录，无法真正测试这一关键能力，因此需要构建更贴近真实场景的评估框架。

Method: (1) 构建APeB（Agent Personalized Benchmark）基准，从用户行为日志中提取数据，将欠指定意图与丰富的交互历史及用户浏览过的候选项配对；(2) 采用多步智能体工作流，评估SOTA LLM在个性化产品搜索中的表现；(3) 通过评分细则（rubric）分析性能差距的归因；(4) 提出VQRA（历史感知的查询精炼管线），通过简单机制改进历史信息利用。

Result: 评估结果表明：LLM在处理显式查询时表现良好，但在需要意图和偏好发现的早期阶段查询中表现挣扎。评分细则分析将这一性能差距主要归因于历史信息利用的低效。VQRA管线带来了稳定一致的性能提升，验证了历史利用模块的重要性。

Conclusion: 个性化智能体亟需专门的历史利用模块来有效处理真实场景中的原始查询。VQRA作为一种简单有效的查询精炼方案，为这一方向提供了有力支撑，未来工作应进一步探索更强大的历史感知机制。

Abstract: LLM-powered agents struggle with personalization when users issue raw, underspecified queries. In this setting, agents must infer latent intent, extract preferences from noisy interaction histories, and select among competing alternatives. Existing benchmarks rarely test this capability, as they often rely on user-refined queries or simplified histories. We introduce personalized product search (PPS), a testbed for agentic personalization under raw queries and diverse histories. We construct Agent Personalized Benchmark (APeB) from action logs, pairing underspecified intents with rich histories and user-viewed candidate items. Evaluating state-of-the-art LLMs with multi-step agent workflows, we find that models handle explicit queries well but struggle with early-stage queries requiring intent and preference discovery. Rubric analysis attributes this gap mainly to ineffective history use. A simple history-aware query-refinement pipeline, VQRA, yields consistent gains, highlighting the need for dedicated history-utilization modules in personalized agents.

</details>


### [85] [Organizational Memory for Agentic Business Process Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03228)
*Lukas Kirchdorfer,Adrian Rebmann,Christian Warmuth,Timotheus Kampik,Theiss Heilker,Gregor Berg*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出为智能体业务流程执行构建"组织记忆"——一个共享的、受治理的、可供智能体消费的组织特定程序性知识参考层，以解决通用LLM缺乏企业专有知识、知识孤岛和规则重复等问题，并在采购场景中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用大语言模型在执行业务流程时缺乏组织特定的知识（如政策、流程模型、标准操作规程等），这些知识分散在面向人类的文档中。虽然可以通过在单个提示或智能体特定的检索设置中编码这些知识，但这种方法在企业中不可扩展，会导致知识孤岛、规则重复，并使跨智能体的一致性更新和学习变得困难。

Method: 作者提出"组织记忆"（organizational memory）的概念，即一个共享的、受治理的、可供智能体消费的演化式组织特定程序性知识参考层。具体包括：(1) 推导该记忆系统的需求；(2) 提出用于知识管理和消费的架构设计；(3) 在采购场景的原型验证中展示其有效性。

Result: 通过基于采购场景的概念验证（proof-of-concept），证明了所提出的组织记忆架构能够有效支持智能体执行业务流程，实现了知识的统一治理、共享消费和一致性更新。

Conclusion: 企业级智能体业务流程执行需要一个超越个体提示和检索设置的组织记忆系统。该共享参考层能够打破知识孤岛、消除规则重复，支持持续的知识演化与跨智能体学习，是实现可扩展、可靠的智能体化业务流程自动化的关键基础设施。

Abstract: LLM-based agents offer new opportunities for automating business process execution beyond the limits of rule-based systems. However, general-purpose LLMs lack the organization-specific knowledge required for reliable execution, which is typically fragmented across human-oriented artifacts such as policies, process models, and standard operating procedures. While such knowledge can technically be encoded in individual prompts or agent-specific retrieval setups, this approach does not scale in enterprises, as it gives rise to knowledge silos and rule duplicates, and makes consistent updates and learning across agents difficult. We argue that this calls for an organizational memory for agentic business process execution: a shared, governed, and agent-consumable reference layer of evolving organization-specific procedural knowledge about how work should be executed. We derive requirements for such a memory, propose an architecture for its curation and consumption, and demonstrate its effectiveness in a proof-of-concept based on a procurement scenario.

</details>


### [86] [Embodied Operators and Benchmarking: Toward Reusable and Deployable Embodied Intelligence Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03283)
*Junwu Xiong,Jiaxuan Gao,Wei Chai,Renxing Chen,Yuzhen Li,Yu Guo,Yucheng Guo,Mingxi Luo,Wenyang Ma,Yiyun Mou,Yifei Zhang,Chen Zhou,Yongjian Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了"具身操作符"（Embodied Operators）的概念，将具身智能系统中的功能模块定义为独立、可组合、可部署的标准化单元，并构建了涵盖五大类别的分类体系及多维度评估基准框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前具身智能系统过度关注端到端策略模型，忽视了将多模态观测、机器人状态等转化为结构化表征与决策的中间功能模块。这些模块缺乏统一的定义边界、标准化接口和独立评估机制，导致系统可复用性、可扩展性差。因此需要将这些模块形式化为"具身操作符"，作为可组合的独立单元进行系统化研究。

Method: （1）定义具身操作符的边界，明确其任务语义、标准化输入输出契约、可部署性、可复用性和多层可优化性五大特征；（2）构建五类操作符分类体系：检测与分割、空间定位与3D理解、手部运动恢复、具身基础模型与任务决策操作符、规划控制与系统支持操作符；（3）提出多维度基准评估框架，涵盖正确性、端到端效率、资源使用、时序稳定性、可移植性、接口兼容性、部署可靠性和下游任务效用八项指标；（4）讨论工作流级操作符加速及开放挑战。

Result: 构建了系统化的具身操作符分类体系，覆盖五大类别，每类总结了代表性功能、技术范式、应用角色及实际局限性；提出了八维度的基准评估框架，为操作符的独立评估提供了统一标准；识别了操作符组合、数据标准化、世界模型、VLA安全、边缘部署等关键开放挑战。

Conclusion: 具身操作符应作为整体可部署组件进行优化和评估，这一范式为构建可复用、可扩展、可验证的具身智能系统奠定了基础。将功能模块从端到端模型中解耦并标准化，是推动具身智能系统工程化发展的关键路径。

Abstract: Embodied intelligence systems require not only end-to-end policy models, but also reusable functional modules that transform multimodal observations, robot states, human demonstrations, and task contexts into structured representations, decisions, trajectories, control references, and system services. This work defines these modules as embodied operators and studies them as independent yet composable units in embodied intelligence pipelines. We clarify their definition boundary, emphasizing task semantics, standardized input-output contracts, deployability, reusability, and multi-layer optimizability. We further construct a taxonomy covering five categories: detection and segmentation, spatial localization and 3D understanding, hand motion recovery, embodied foundation models and task-decision operators, and planning, control, and system support operators. For each category, we summarize representative functions, technical paradigms, application roles, and practical limitations. Beyond taxonomy, we propose a multi-dimensional benchmark framework that evaluates embodied operators in terms of correctness, end-to-end efficiency, resource usage, temporal stability, portability, interface compatibility, deployment reliability, and downstream task utility. We also discuss workflow-level operator acceleration and open challenges in operator composition, data standardization, world models, VLA safety, edge deployment, and real-world application value. Overall, this work argues that embodied operators should be optimized and evaluated as holistic deployable components, providing a foundation for reusable, scalable, and verifiable embodied intelligence systems.

### [87] [Reflective Dialogue or Prompt Refinement? Effects of Tutor Scaffolding on Students' Independent LLM Use for Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03303)
*Jerome Brender,Laila El-Hamamsy,Kim Uittenhove,Aitor Perez,Patrick Jermann,Francesco Mondada,Engin Bumbacher*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究对比了两种LLM导师（苏格拉底式引导SG vs. 提示精炼PR）对研究生学习的影响。结果显示：短期内两者任务表现相似，但SG导师在长期学习收益和培养"理解驱动型"提问策略方面显著优于PR导师，尽管SG被学生感知为效率较低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM在教育中展现个性化支持潜力，但学习效果取决于学生如何与之互动。当前缺乏对不同LLM导师设计如何塑造学生的提问实践、学习成果及后续自主使用LLM能力的实证研究。

Method: 在研究生移动机器人课程中开展两阶段实验：(1) 66名学生被分配使用SG导师或PR导师，为期6周；(2) 随后52名学生使用无约束LLM完成3周课程项目。通过对比两组在不同阶段的任务表现、提问模式、学习收益及LLM使用策略进行分析。

Result: (1) 在引导使用阶段，SG和PR两组任务表现和提问模式相似；(2) SG组学生在后期阶段学习收益更高；(3) 在无约束LLM使用阶段，SG组更倾向采用"理解驱动型"提问策略，该策略可预测更高理解水平；(4) SG导师被学生感知为效率较低。

Conclusion: 苏格拉底式引导虽然短期内看似效率不高，但能够培养学生长期"学会用LLM学习"的元能力——即发展出理解驱动的提问策略，这对LLM教育导师的设计具有重要启示。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) can provide personalized support in learning, several studies have raised concerns regarding their use in education. Importantly, learning depends on how students engage with LLMs. This study examined how two types of LLM-based tutors shape students' prompting practices, learning, and subsequent LLM-use: a Socratic-Guidance (SG) tutor, which structures interaction through dialogic questioning, and a Prompt-Refinement (PR) tutor that guides the formulation of effective prompts. We conducted a two-phase study in a graduate-level mobile robotics course: 66 students used either the SG or PR tutor during a 6-week intervention, followed by 52 students using an unconstrained LLM during a 3-week course project. Results show that while the SG- and PR tutors led to similar task performance and prompting patterns during guided use, they differ in learning outcomes and later LLM-use. SG-students, relative to PR-student, achieved higher learning gains in later sessions, and were more likely to adopt understanding-driven prompting strategies, which are predictive of higher understanding, when using an unconstrained LLM. Although learners perceived the SG tutor as less efficient, the findings suggest that Socratic guidance supports the development of students' capacity to learn with LLMs over time, highlighting its importance for LLM tutor design.
